Flower Association's Evil Deeds: Cutting Off the Heads of the Dead to Pray for Dreams

The Deceased Was Originally a Victim of the Flower Association

Zhang A'yu and Others Inevitably Offended Against Humanity

At around 4:00 AM yesterday morning, when the sky was not yet light, a Chinese policeman on duty at the Meibai Road intersection of Jing'an Temple Road saw a rickshaw puller frantically running eastwards, with an old man of about fifty years old sitting in the rickshaw, carrying a circular package by his side. The policeman, finding it suspicious that the rickshaw was being pulled frantically in the deep night, stopped the rickshaw and questioned the origin and destination of the passengers. The man in the rickshaw appeared panicked upon being stopped and gave evasive answers. The policeman ordered the package to be opened, but the passenger stubbornly refused to let go. After repeated coercion by the policeman, he finally relented and released the package. The policeman unwrapped it, revealing a horrifying human head, smeared with fresh blood, with eyes wide open and teeth bared. The policeman immediately brought the passenger and the rickshaw puller to the Jing'an Temple Road police station. Under strict interrogation by the police chief, the passenger identified himself as Zhang A'yu, from Yuyao, aged sixty, residing at No. 8 of Yangshupu Baidaitou, working as a small fruit vendor. He confessed that he and six or seven friends were fond of gambling on Flower Associations.

They recently learned that there was a new corpse in the Yizhong Cemetery in the French Concession of West Shanghai. The deceased was also fond of Flower Associations during his lifetime, but after his family fortune was depleted, he committed suicide by hanging. The group believed that if they could obtain the corpse's head to pray for dreams, it would surely be effective, but all were too timid to go. Only Zhang was relatively brave, so the group insisted on pushing Zhang to go to the Yizhong Cemetery yesterday morning, cut off the head of the new corpse, and carry it back wrapped up, so that they could pray for dreams. After obtaining the confession, the police chief immediately inquired about the names and addresses of his accomplices. Zhang confessed to the names Wang Zhilun, Tang Laosan, She A'er, Lu Shunchang, Sun Deli, Wang Zhangshi, and Gao Risheng, among others, all residing in Baidaitou. The police chief immediately dispatched policemen to arrest them at their addresses and seized a murder weapon as evidence, awaiting transfer to the court for interrogation.

Liu Chongwu and Others Convicted

Liu Sentenced to Seven Years of Imprisonment

Liu Chongwu and others, for using bombs and handguns to deal with unscrupulous merchants privately selling Japanese goods, repeatedly staged tragic incidents of injury and death. They were arrested by detectives Zhao Bingkun and others from the Public Concession Police Department, and firearms and bombs were seized. The Bureau of Law of the Public Works Department, based on charges of premeditated murder, attempted murder, obstruction of freedom, and private possession of military weapons, filed a public lawsuit with the First Special District Court. Judge Qian Wenji has already held a trial and concluded the investigation, with a verdict awaiting announcement. Yesterday morning, the date for the announcement of the verdict arrived. Undertaking Chinese and Western detectives escorted the six defendants, Liu Chongwu, Pan Hongsheng, Cao Songshou, Tian Shuiyang, Zhu Liangkang, Hua Zhida, and others, along with the evidence, to the court. At 9:00 AM, Judge Qian ascended the second courtroom and ordered the six to be brought forward. After inquiring about their names, ages, places of origin, and occupations, he announced the judgment. Liu Chongwu was sentenced to six years and eight months of imprisonment for the crime of murdering Wang Yirong, and six months of imprisonment for the crime of private possession of military weapons, to be served concurrently for a total of seven years of imprisonment. Pan Hongsheng was sentenced to three months of imprisonment for the crime of private possession of military weapons. Cao Songshou was sentenced to three months of imprisonment for the crime of private possession of military weapons, and three months of imprisonment for the crime of obstruction of freedom, to be served concurrently for a total of four months of imprisonment. Tian Shuiyang was sentenced to three months of imprisonment for the crime of private possession of military weapons. Zhu Erkang and Hua Zhida were each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for the crime of obstruction of freedom. Tian, Zhu, and Hua were each granted a two-year suspended sentence. The firearms and ammunition were confiscated. After the judgment, Judge Qian briefly stated the reasons for the judgment, generally saying that regarding the case of Wang Zhengtao of the Maotai Foreign Goods Store on Xinzha Road being shot and killed, there was no evidence to prove that the defendants were responsible. Moreover, Cao Songshou had already left the scene when the incident occurred. Since the murderer in that case has not yet been apprehended, it should be judged separately in the future. As for Wang Yirong of the Yuyuan Heng Foreign Goods Company on Hankou Road being shot and killed by Liu Chongwu, not only was the evidence substantial, but Liu had also confessed. However, according to Liu's confession, Wang Yirong tried to grab him, so he opened fire. Therefore, his motive for killing was temporary and not premeditated, which is evident in the circumstances. According to the law, the crime of murder must be punished by death, or at least ten years of imprisonment. Considering that the defendant violated the criminal law due to the patriotic movement, which is not without justification, the sentence has been reduced by one-third. The other defendants committed obstruction of freedom, although it was not just once, it can only be regarded as a continuous act and dealt with as such. As for Tian Shuiyang, Zhu Erkang, Hua Zhida, and others, their crimes are light and they have no illegal activities in their past. This time, they were caught in the criminal net because of patriotism, so considering the original situation, a suspended sentence is declared. Judge Qian then informed Liu and others that if they were not satisfied with this judgment, they could appeal to the Second Higher Branch Court. The police station's lawyer, Wang Yaotang, then requested that the three people who were granted a suspended sentence also be temporarily detained in order to consider whether to appeal. The court approved it, and the six people, including Liu, were still taken back to the police station for detention.

A Foreman Revives After Death

Three Murderers Sent to Court

Yang Zhenqing, from Anhui, residing at No. 10 Meihe Lane, Shanzhong Road, French Concession,

worked as a foreman at a construction factory on Jing'an Temple Road and had considerable savings. Jiang Zhaolin, a fellow villager, borrowed 80 yuan from him and gave him a bond. On November 7th of last year, Jiang invited Yang to Jiang Changgui's home in Jiangwan Jiangjing Temple to dine, and mentioned that Zhao Yangfu owed him money and would return it immediately. They then drank wine and chatted. Benji Zhao also came, so Jiang Zhaolin, Jiang Changgui, Jiang Yonggui, Zhao Yangfu, and a woman accompanied Yang to drink wine and dine. Afterwards, they paid him 80 yuan, and Yang returned the IOU. It was already very late, and he went home immediately, with Jiang and others accompanying him. In a remote area, Yang Zhenqing was stabbed wildly by them, resulting in a knife wound to the head and one to the abdomen. The silver dollars were also robbed. At this time, Yang was already dead. The perpetrators thought he was dead, which could be said without risk. Unexpectedly, after an hour, Yang Zhenqing gradually revived, but the pain was unbearable, and his moans were incessant. A patrol policeman from the Fifth District, Fifth Station happened to pass by, saw him, and sent him to the station, and then to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment. He has gradually been able to move and his mind is clear, so he filed a complaint with the station, which sent police to arrest Jiang Changgui, Jiang Yonggui, and Zhao Yangfu. They were taken to the Municipal Public Security Bureau and transferred to the local court for thorough investigation.

In addition, the Shenjiamen Chamber of Commerce and fishermen from Fujian and Zhejiang telegraphed, "Having heard of your honorable appointment as Commissioner for the Protection of Foreign Waters in Zhejiang, you will be familiar with the job, and we deeply rejoice. Congratulations."

Female Performer's Disaster: Acquainted with Two Men, a Bloodshed Occurs in the Painter's Room

A Thug Attacks with a Stick, the Painter Defends with an Axe

As a Result, the Thug is Seriously Injured and Dies Before Receiving Treatment

Zhang Yanxia, a Kunqu opera performer in the Dajing Troupe at the Sun Sun Theater on Nanjing Road, originally from Changzhou, aged thirty-two, has been with the troupe as a female martial artist. She has had a long-standing affair with Meng Lanting, a painter from Beiping who specializes in stage scenery. Meng is advanced in age, and Zhang, disliking his age, became involved with Zhang A'gao, a young and strong thug. Although Meng knew about it, he never interfered. However, Zhang considered the performer his territory and warned her that if she had any relationship with a third party, he would confront them as an enemy. At 3:30 PM the day before yesterday, Meng was working in the backstage scenery room when Zhang A'gao suddenly entered, leading to a fight. Li Hoxi and Tang Xianming, who were outside the room, heard the noise and went to check. Because the door was locked, they could not see what was happening inside. They broke down the door and found Zhang A'gao lying in a pool of blood, with several injuries to his head and face. Meng Lanting was sitting silently in a corner, his sleeves stained with blood. After repeated questioning, he admitted that Zhang had forcibly borrowed money from him. When he refused, Zhang attacked him with an iron rod. In self-defense, he grabbed an axe to resist. At that moment, the Yueyuan inspector arrived and summoned the police to arrest Meng and detain him at the Laozha Police Station. Zhang A'gao was taken to the hospital, but his injuries were fatal. He died before receiving treatment. His body was taken to the Felun Road morgue to await an official autopsy. The police chief ordered detectives to investigate the circumstances of the incident. Suspecting that Zhang Yanxia was the source of the trouble, they arrested her at No. 1255 Edward Road. Yesterday morning, she and Meng Lanting were taken to the First Special District Court. The murder weapon, an axe, two iron rods, and blood-stained clothing were submitted as evidence. Judge Qian questioned them. Police lawyer Ru BaoYi presented the situation of the case, stating that Meng Lanting was being prosecuted for murder under Article 282 of the Criminal Law. Whether Zhang Yanxia was involved was still under investigation. He requested temporary detention. Meng confessed that since Zhang A'gao became involved with Zhang Yanxia, he had repeatedly borrowed money from him. He borrowed 100 yuan last year and had not yet returned it. Yesterday he wanted to borrow 50 yuan. When I had no money to pay, he hit me with an iron bar. My left wrist was injured, so I took an axe to defend myself. At that time, I was mentally confused and did not care about the consequences. Zhang Yanxia testified that since she became involved with Zhang A'gao, he had extorted countless amounts of money from her. Whenever he ran out of money, he would come and demand it. Even if she had pawned everything, he would still find a way to satisfy his desires. She did not know why he clashed with Meng this time. After reviewing the testimonies, Judge Qian ordered Meng Lanting to be remanded and Zhang Yanxia to be released, pending an autopsy. It is heard that the corpse will be examined by a prosecutor from the First Special District Court this morning.

The Municipal Government Announces the Revised Regulations for Registration of Construction Factories

The Shanghai Municipal Government announced the revised Shanghai Municipal Regulations for Registration of Construction Factories yesterday. The original text is as follows: Article 1: All construction factories, construction companies, carpentry businesses, etc. operating within the municipal area of this city shall apply for registration with the Public Works Bureau in accordance with these regulations. Those who are not registered shall not be allowed to contract construction projects within the city. Article 2: Applicants for registration shall obtain a registration form from the Public Works Bureau, fill out two copies in the prescribed format, and have it certified by two fellow businesses, with their business seals affixed to the form. A registration fee of two yuan and a stamp tax of one yuan shall be submitted. After review and qualification, a registration certificate shall be issued. Those who do not qualify shall have the registration fee and stamp tax returned. Article 3: Construction factories, etc. that have not registered and privately contract construction projects shall be fined up to 100 yuan by the Public Works Bureau after investigation, and shall be ordered to register. Article 4: If a registrant has one of the following circumstances, the Public Works Bureau may, depending on the circumstances, impose a suspension of business for one to ten months. If the circumstances are serious, the registration may be cancelled and the registration certificate recovered: (1) Failing to construct in accordance with the drawings approved by the Public Works Bureau; (2) Reducing materials, resulting in danger; (3) Repeatedly violating regulations despite warnings; (4) Impersonating another person's registration number or lending the registration certificate to others. Article 5: Those who have been suspended from business for more than three months and those whose registration has been cancelled shall be publicly announced by the Public Works Bureau in the newspaper at any time. Article 6: When obtaining a construction permit from the Public Works Bureau, the registration certificate of the contracting engineer shall be submitted, and the Public Works Bureau shall fill in the area and permit number in the permit application form attached to the certificate, and affix a seal for return. If the contractor has not yet been hired at the time of obtaining the permit, the above procedures shall be completed before construction begins. Article 7: Registrants shall submit the registration certificate for verification once a year. The Public Works Bureau shall issue a new permit application form within the certificate. The date of submission for verification shall be from July 1st for one month. A handling fee of one yuan shall be paid for exceeding the time limit. Those who exceed the time limit by more than one year shall re-register. Article 8: Registrants who voluntarily cease business or change their address shall notify the Public Works Bureau in writing. Article 9: If the registration certificate is lost, it shall be immediately reported in the newspaper and a request shall be submitted to the Public Works Bureau for a replacement, along with a handling fee of one yuan and a stamp tax of one yuan. Article 10: These regulations may be amended at any time if there are any matters not covered. Article 11: These regulations shall take effect from the date of promulgation by the Municipal Government.

Large Amount of Opium on the Xing Shi Steamer

A Total of More Than Eight Thousand Taels

Seized in the Fire Hold

The Xing Shi steamer of the Sanbei Company, coming from Hankou to Shanghai this time, had a large batch of opium seized on board. The following is a detailed account of what the reporter learned from the investigation:

Special Tax Office Receives Report

The Changjiang steamer Xing Shi of the Sanbei Steamship Company is currently chartered and travels between Hankou, Nanjing, and Yichang. On the 7th of this month, the steamer returned to Hankou from the upper Yangtze and was to sail to Shanghai. The Lianghu Special Tax Office in Hankou had previously received a confidential report stating that the steamer had loaded a large amount of opium in Yichang, intending to transport it to Shanghai for unloading. Upon receiving the report, the Special Tax Office remained silent and went to inspect the ship upon arrival.

Administrator Assists in Seizure

Chartered commercial ships do not load commercial goods or carry passengers, so they should not be inspected. The management right of the ship does not belong to the shipping company but to the special commissioner. When the Xing Shi docked, the Customs Division of the Lianghu Special Tax Office immediately went to the ship to visit the ship administrator, Li Wenhu, and explained that there was a huge amount of opium on board, smuggled in and intended to be transported to Shanghai under the guise of charter transport. Li Wenhu, upon hearing this, believed that this matter was related to his reputation, agreed to the inspection, and provided assistance in the search.

Large Amount of Opium Seized

The entire team of inspectors from the Special Tax Office, together with the administrator, boarded the ship at 11:00 AM on the 7th to search for smuggled opium. They searched separately, and at 11:40 AM, they seized dozens of large and small bags of smuggled opium in the fire hold of the ship's engine room. The Special Tax Office reported that the total weight was about eight thousand and several hundred taels. They also said that some of it may have been leaked out, because according to confidential reports, it was more than this number. It is thought that it was transported to other ships and leaked out.

Strict Prohibition on All Yangtze Steamers

After this case occurred, the investigation of smugglers revealed that most of them were being smuggled by stokers and others from the fire hold. After the incident, they all fled. According to regulations, the ship could only be released after the main culprits were caught. Because the Xing Shi is currently chartered, the ship administrator reported to the military, while one side was arresting the suspects. Yesterday, letters were sent to various shipping companies, requesting them to instruct all Yangtze steamer crew members to strictly prohibit smuggling prohibited goods. In the future, if found again, the ship owners and others will be held responsible. The seized large amount of opium was confiscated by the Special Tax Office.

Foreign Pickpockets Active in Shanghai During the New Year

Male and Female Thieves Are All Dressed in Elegant Attire and Are Very Respectable

Surrounding a Guest to Wish Them Happy New Year, Stealing Their Money in an Instant

Three Guests Lost a Great Deal of Money in a Certain Wine Shop in the Western District

...Most of the Pickpockets Are Russians...

The North China Daily News reports that on New Year's Eve, several foreign male and female thieves, dressed in elegant attire and wearing evening gowns, entered and exited banquets, entertainment venues, and used their pickpocketing skills. Almost all of the well-known clubhouses, wine shops, and hotel dance halls in this city were patronized by them. When the police received the report, they sent people to strictly guard various public recreation areas, and these uninvited guests were driven away. According to the police, there are currently about 60 foreign pickpockets, most of whom are Russians, who frequently travel to and from Shanghai, Hong Kong, Dalian, Harbin, and other places. Each time they arrive in a port, they stay for several weeks to several months. This New Year's Eve happened to be in Shanghai. It is heard that in a certain clubhouse, the money in the pockets of three male guests disappeared, and one female guest also lost valuable items in her handbag. It is suspected that it was stolen by two men and two women. In a certain wine shop, they also patronized and surrounded a guest to wish them a happy New Year. A few minutes later, the guest suddenly felt the money in his pocket disappear. Upon searching, the suspicious men and a woman had already escaped in the meantime. Only one woman was detained, but due to a lack of evidence, she was released. The men and women were all wearing evening gowns and beautiful clothes, so no one initially suspected that they were skilled pickpockets. A larger pickpocketing case occurred in a certain wine shop in the western district. A gentleman lost 300 US dollars. Two other guests were also victimized, with a total loss of around 2,500 yuan for the three of them. It is heard that a female guest also had 300 yuan stolen in a certain hotel near the Bund. Thanks to the alertness of the staff and detectives in the two major wine shops in the French Concession, it is heard that nothing was lost. In one, a certain manager saw two men and a woman acting suspiciously and immediately asked others to leave. In another wine shop, detectives drove several men and women out. There may be several other minor cases, but because the victims do not want to publicize them, they are still unknown.

Rickshaw Puller Crushed to Death by Car

Su Fengshun, from Yancheng, aged 55, residing at No. 29 Meilan Lane, Beile Road, French Concession, made a living pulling a rickshaw. At 6:10 PM last night, while traveling along Lafayette Road, a white-license car with the number 12109 sped towards him. Unable to avoid it, Su Fengshun was knocked to the ground, suffering injuries to his head and abdomen. An Annamese policeman No. 217 from the Songshan Road Police Station rushed to the scene, recorded the car number, and immediately sent the injured man to Renji Hospital for treatment. He died at 10:30 PM.

The inspection results are hereby announced as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible notes issued: 41,365,682 silver dollars, including: silver dollar notes: 37,529,833 silver dollars; subsidiary currency: 3,835,849 silver dollars; total amount of convertible note reserve fund: 41,365,682 silver dollars, including: cash reserve: 33,976,682 silver dollars. The cash reserve is comprised of: 30,224,295 silver dollars stored in the bank's issuing vault; 1,923,282 silver dollars stored in branches in various ports; 1,829,105 silver dollars deposited with fellow banks; and a guarantee reserve equivalent to 7,389,000 silver dollars. (B) Total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued: 425,000 customs gold units; total amount of customs gold convertible note reserve fund: 425,000 customs gold units. This reserve fund includes: 17 [amount missing in original text] U.S. dollars, deposited with fellow banks in this port, priced at 40 [units missing in original text] equivalent to 425,000 customs gold units. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Note Regulations, the cash reserve should be 60% and the guarantee reserve should be 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby issued. January 10th, 1933, Central Bank Board of Supervisors.

Letters to the Editor

Dear Editor, Today I read in your newspaper the news item about Duan Zhiyun, an engineer of the Yizhong Real Estate Company, fraudulently claiming 3,000 yuan. However, this person is not an engineer of our company. He was temporarily borrowed by our company as a clerk. Please publish this letter in your newspaper's Letters to the Editor section to correct the record. Sincerely, Yizhong Real Estate Company, January 11, 1933.

Dear Editor, Yesterday, the news in this city reported that a gangster fight with shooting occurred at the Huaiyang Teahouse in Zhabei, and members of the Security Corps participated in the incident. This does not match the facts. It was found that on that night, First Platoon Leader Luo Wenjie was leading his corps members on patrol when they were informed that a car was parked on Meiwei Road, attempting to kidnap a certain Chen. The platoon leader and others immediately rushed to investigate and saw the car parked empty on the side of the road. After inquiring, they learned that it had been there for a long time. Soon after, the chauffeur arrived, and while they were questioning him, Wang Agen and Chen Shiying came pulling and tugging. They immediately questioned them. Chen Shiying claimed that the gangster Wang Agen had a grudge against him and had now gathered a group to invite him to a "tea talk" in an attempt to scare and kidnap him. Wang Agen, on the other hand, claimed that Chen Shiying had flirted with the wife of his friend Fang on the road. Fang was indignant and invited them to a "tea talk" at the Huaiyang Building. He was only there to help, because Chen Shiying was unwilling to go, so he pulled him along. It was not kidnapping. At that time, the police on duty at the post thought that the chauffeur and the car had to be taken to the district. Platoon Leader Luo immediately accompanied them to the Fourth District, and at the same time, fearing that the gangsters would gather at the teahouse to cause trouble, he ordered several corps members to accompany Wang Agen and Chen Shiying to the building to investigate. Unexpectedly, upon arriving at the teahouse, dozens of gangsters, without asking questions, swarmed forward. The corps members, because they were outnumbered, were not only injured, but also had a pistol taken from them. However, in order to be cautious, even though they were injured, they did not fire their weapons. At that time, Jin Xianglin and Xiao Wenbin, members of the Eighth Platoon, happened to pass by and immediately reported to the police on duty. The police saw the surging crowd and could not dissuade them, so they fired two warning shots into the air. The gangsters then slightly calmed down, and Wang Agen and Chen Shi,

Ying were detained. Because the corps members were on official duty to the scene to suppress the disturbance, they did not dodge and immediately went to the district together. This is the real situation at the time. In addition to sending a letter to the Public Security Bureau, we are correspondingly sending this letter, requesting that you correct the record as soon as possible. Sincerely, Shanghai City Security Corps Management Committee, January 11.

Dear Editor, The news item "Recent Events at the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company" in your newspaper on January 11 contained the following statement: "The Municipal Government of this city, upon seeing a report in the daily newspaper that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company had borrowed money from Jardine Matheson, felt it was quite peculiar and specially sent Wang Shaozhai to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company yesterday to meet with General Manager Liu." Sincerely, Information Office of the Municipal Government's News Department, January 11.

Dear Editor, In your newspaper's news column on the 8th of this month, there was a report on the opening of the Longmao Yarn Factory case, stating that Zhang Geng had absconded, which does not match the facts. The court hearing was on the 6th. It happened that my appointed lawyer, Shan Yuhua, had returned to his hometown due to bereavement, and Lawyer Zha Renwei had also returned to his hometown for the New Year. On the 5th, I telegraphed to inquire and learned that they had not returned. The staff of the two law firms, fearing that they would not be able to attend the court and delay the debate, specially requested a postponement. On the morning of the 6th, the opposing lawyer, Wu Linkun, also came to my place, requesting a settlement, and also said that he could request a postponement. Therefore, in the afternoon, I rushed to handle other important matters first, and then rushed to the court, just in time for the court to adjourn. I met the opposing parties and Mr. Zha, who told me that he had arrived on the early train, and that the court had rescheduled the hearing for next Monday. I did not expect that the opposing lawyer, Wu, would take the opportunity to make such a deep-seated insinuation. I had already filed a counterclaim in this case and was waiting to engage in a legal battle with the opposing party. I thought that, as a general rule, those who resort to criminal intimidation for other purposes should be warned. What need was there for me to abscond? This kind of news strategy is not worth mentioning, but it concerns my commercial reputation, so I must ask your newspaper to correct the record solemnly. Please publish this letter. Sincerely, Lawyer Zha Renwei, representing Zhang Bingjun, January 11, 1933.

Special Feature

Preface to "Easy Methods for Curing Lung Disease" by Ding Fubao

My family, starting with my sister-in-law Di, died of pulmonary tuberculosis. After that, my father, my younger sister, and two nieces also died of this disease one after another. I have also suffered from lung disease repeatedly and am unable to protect myself. Alas, the scourge of lung disease has greatly afflicted my family! And among my friends, Fan Xiaolian Suxing, Wang Shuchang Maiqing, Gao Shangshe Zhong'an, Lian Shangshe Yiqing, and Zhengsheng, etc., also died of lung disease. Although our country does not have death statistics tables that can be used for verification, judging from what I have seen and heard in recent decades, lung disease accounts for about one-seventh of all deaths, or perhaps the actual number is even higher. Tuberculosis is truly a great enemy of mankind. Moreover, those who suffer from lung disease are mostly young people in the prime of life. Speaking from a family perspective, it is a very tragic event. Speaking from a national perspective, it is also a great misfortune. Therefore, when we hear the diagnosis of lung disease, we become depressed, thinking that the outcome of this disease must be bad, no different from being sentenced to death. But we do not know that this is a big mistake of the world. Lung disease is actually an easy disease to cure. If treated early, there is no one who will not be cured. Taking my own experience as an example, you can know that lung disease is not to be feared. I have been ill since childhood, with a weak body, small wrists, soft and weak muscles, chronic cough with phlegm, indigestion, and a pale complexion. Gu Junxiaodong said that I would definitely die of illness in the future. This was my condition before I was twenty years old. Extending to the age of twenty-eight, I came to Shanghai. The weakness of my body was still the same. If I walked one or two li, I would be out of breath and exhausted, and my spirit would also be exhausted. Moreover, I had not been able to lie on my right side for more than ten years. If I lay on my right side, I would feel very short of breath. Therefore, every night I could only sleep comfortably on my left side. Chinese medicine books say that those who can only sleep on one side will surely die. At that time, my weight was less than ninety pounds. A life insurance doctor examined my body and diagnosed me with stage 2 pulmonary tuberculosis. He did not dare to insure my life for ten years and advised me to take medicine. I did not believe him, so I sought out the methods of exhaling the old and inhaling the new and stretching the body like a bear, etc., from Hua Tuo of the Three Kingdoms period, which is what is called the Five Animal Frolics. However, this method of exercise is too vigorous and may injure the internal organs, so it is not suitable for a sick body. I learned from its meaning and improved it. At the beginning, the exercise was very slight and did not require any strength, so even the very weak could handle it. I also practiced meditation, concentrating on the "xuanguan" point, calming my mind and qi, putting down all past, present, and future affairs, and not allowing myself to think about them, so that my spirit could rest. I also adopted various therapeutic methods such as sunlight, air, and diet, all of which were in line with scientific principles. At that time, my self-confidence was very strong, thinking that my illness would definitely be cured, and I could use a firm, unyielding, courageous, and diligent spirit to fight off the demons of illness for decades to come. My single-minded, stubborn, and laughable persistence was like this. After practicing for two years, my sick body was indeed cured. At the age of thirty, I was hired by the Imperial University of Peking to be a teacher of arithmetic, physiology, and hygiene. The daily coursework was very busy, and I did not take a sick leave for almost three years. After that, I returned to Shanghai to engage in publishing and to treat people for more than twenty years. This year, I am already sixty years old. I can sleep comfortably on both sides when lying down. Although my beard and hair are white, my body is still strong. In these thirty years, I have never had a day when I had to decline guests due to illness or be bedridden and unable to get up. I had been compiling the "Shuowen Gu Lin" for more than a thousand volumes and was too busy to treat people for several years. Now that the "Gu Lin" has been published for a long time, and the "Gu Lin Supplements," which are 170 volumes, have also been published, I have a lot of free time every day. I plan to personally teach those who are physically weak like I was in my youth, or those who are middle-aged with anemia, qi deficiency, indigestion, neurasthenia, or excessive indulgence in lust, as well as those who are at risk of lung disease, or those who are already in the early stages of lung disease, or the elderly with declining physical strength, difficulty walking, chronic cough, etc., regardless of gender, can all learn. It will be effective in a month, and greatly effective in three months. If you can be determined and unyielding, you will surely be able to achieve the goal of preventing disease, without a doubt. Moreover, it is not only to prevent disease. After studying for several years, your work spirit will surely surpass that of ordinary people by several times, and others will only be able to sigh in admiration. My natural endowment is very poor, far inferior to that of ordinary people. After the age of sixty, I do not know if I can be as healthy as I was after the age of thirty. Thinking of this, I dare not stop my disease prevention and recuperation methods for even a day. Are there also those who, on the lonely shore of the wilderness river, hear the wind and rise up? Now, in addition to compiling the disease prevention and recuperation methods, I still have some free time, so I have compiled a book on easy methods for curing lung disease, using very simple language, in the form of questions and answers. Those with lung disease should implement it according to the law, and engage in a long-term resistance and annihilation of tuberculosis. Even after the inherent health has been restored, all the efforts made cannot be interrupted to prevent the recurrence of lung disease. Alas, if this book had been completed forty years ago, my relatives and old friends would surely have benefited from it. Why would they have been so afflicted by tuberculosis and withered away like this? Now that the proofreading is complete, touching on past events, I am filled with emotion and shed tears as I write this preface. Ding Fubao Zhonghu of Wuxi, January 1933, wrote this in the Gu Lin Study in the previous year.

Reader's Forum

The Panic Cycle Law and the "Anti-Imperialist" Problem

丨丨Letter from Mr. Wang Xiping丨丨

Reporter: Your newspaper's editorial "How Will 1933 Be?" in the past two days is like a morning rooster in the current world of opinion, and like a beacon in your newspaper. After reading it, I cannot help but sigh, "A rare and valuable voice!" However, there are still several points that Mr. Nai has said that I, in my ignorance, cannot understand. Therefore, I raise them below, respectfully seeking enlightenment: (1) Mr. Nai said: "The need for institutional change is just like the need for life to go through birth, old age, sickness, and death and be replaced. Therefore, the so-called 'panic cycle' is not a merry-go-round-style cycle, but a spiral-style advancement. 'Time flies and people age,' and the panic cycle is also constantly urging. The current system goes from infancy to full bloom, and from full bloom to decline. The fact that the current system must come to an end under a certain panic is something that we know is inevitable by looking back at the history of human society and observing the general course of human life." I completely agree with this statement. It is praiseworthy that your newspaper, which is usually so mature and prudent, has such a courageous statement exposing the inevitable fate of the current society. First, it shows that your newspaper's reporter has already stepped into the periphery of the new era. Second, it proves that the darkness of the times is about to reach the place where it intersects with light. This is something worth celebrating. But Mr. Nai also said: "We do not want to fundamentally deny the panic cycle law, but only need to modify it." Looking at his so-called modification, it is roughly as quoted above, recognizing that the panic cycle law is "not a merry-go-round style," but "a spiral style." The implication is that the previous claim that the panic cycle law was "a merry-go-round style" rather than a spiral style. Is Mr. Nai's statement really accurate? (2) Mr. Nai said: "The meaning of sacrifice is clear, and the value of suffering has been determined. Then we should sharpen ourselves to be ready, sing praises and approach, and rise up to fight to the death with the invading countries. The anti-imperialist struggles of colonies and semi-colonies are now the only option left, a desperate move. Then the only thing to do is to rise up together, and engage in hand-to-hand combat,..." These exciting words are naturally what we young people all want to say but cannot say, or say but cannot say with such pain and generosity. However, assuming that we now want to implement anti-imperialist work, implement what Mr. Nai instructed, "rise up together," I am afraid that before we even "engage in hand-to-hand combat," everyone will have already been "arrested." Then where will you have the opportunity to "engage in hand-to-hand combat"? In my humble opinion, if China does not want to implement anti-imperialism, but only talks about it, sends telegrams, and writes articles, then that is fine. But if we really want to implement anti-imperialism, then there must be three preconditions: unconditionally realize the three major freedoms of a democratic country; unconditionally lift the ban on political parties; and unconditionally grant amnesty to political prisoners. If one of these three conditions cannot be met, then anti-imperialism is just an empty lie. Know that throughout ancient and modern history, there is no nation or country that has turned the majority of its people into a state of apathy, afraid to even fart, and can meet the foreign powers on the battlefield. Therefore, I believe that the people must demand that the government, or the government should automatically and immediately realize the above three preconditions before there can be any talk of "anti-imperialism" or "resistance against Japan." What does your newspaper's reporter think?

Reporter's note: Mr. Wang's letter has such a detailed discussion of the editorial by Mr. Nai of this newspaper, which shows his spirit of studying on a regular basis. I admire him very much! In addition to hoping that Mr. Nai, the reporter of this newspaper, will reply to the two points raised, if any of you readers have any insights, please also send a letter to discuss them.

Discussion on the Issue of Resuming Diplomatic Relations Between China and the Soviet Union

丨丨Letter from Mr. Fang Juehua丨丨

(The original letter from Mr. Wu Lengqiu appeared in this column on December 28th)

Regarding the various questions raised by Mr. Wu Lengqiu's communication to the reporter, singling out the question of "Who wanted to sever relations?" and "Who wants to resume relations?" as the core of all issues is indeed accurate. In my opinion, the severance of relations with Russia was caused partly by the Chinese people's lack of sufficient understanding of the Soviet Union, and partly because our diplomacy was not proactive, leading to a blind severance. Now, the Chinese people have a considerable understanding of it. At the same time, in the diplomatic field, due to the severe national crisis, the masks of the imperialists have been torn off, and we have realized the mistake of previously flattering the imperialists. Therefore, we resolutely resumed diplomatic relations. As to whether we will sever relations again in the future, it all depends on whether the government can maintain its spirit of truly independent diplomacy. In short, we don't need to be overjoyed or fearful about resuming diplomatic relations with Russia. The current national crisis still needs to be resolved by our own strength. In the 20th century, closing the door cannot prevent foreign aggression. The attitude we should adopt is that it is better to have one less enemy, and friends should not be used by the enemy. The impact of severing relations with Russia was that revolutionary diplomacy was in an isolated position, but it won applause internationally. The imperialists all said that China was indeed lovable and understood their intentions deeply. Now that relations have been resumed, they have learned that the giant of the East is gradually awakening, and therefore harbor a sense of suspicion, fearing that the two great nations will join hands and pose a powerful threat to their capitalism. But can we really stand up because of this? In my opinion, it's just a decadent and sickly ghost getting an injection of stimulants!

Japanese Prostitutes

— Qia

It seems somewhat irrelevant to talk about Japanese prostitutes amidst the anti-Japanese clamor; however, according to friends who have returned from Japan, Japanese prostitutes never offer non-Japanese tobacco and alcohol to their customers, which seems worthy of attention. Looking back at China, where imported goods are respected, prostitutes are indeed compulsory salespeople for foreign goods, but how can we not be surprised that even people who are looked down upon take using foreign goods as a sign of extravagance!

Why are Japanese prostitutes so patriotic? Because they already have faith and determination in their own domestic goods, and it is also due to the shifting social customs, but they would rather use second-rate Japanese goods and firmly reject non-Japanese goods.

Tobacco and alcohol are originally consumable items, and trying tobacco and alcohol in brothels is especially outside the bounds of normal life; but by analogy, before we eliminate the deep-rooted notion that imported goods are better, if the first step is not to be ashamed of using second-rate domestic goods, and if we can consistently do so, we can indeed recover a portion of the leakage from the huge per capita statistical charts.

How Should Domestic Goods Find a Way Out Under Heavy Oppression (Part 2)

— Du Chongda

In the course of the collapse of the agricultural economy, the industrial economy has gradually emerged, and today most cities have entered the realm of capitalism, and even the rural economy is gradually changing its nature. However, this kind of change is created by the forces of the capitalist economy, not by natural change. Therefore, our country's so-called national industry is invariably manipulated and controlled by advanced capitalist countries, struggling to survive, relying on others for a living, and in an extremely miserable situation.

Especially since the tide of the economic panic in July 1929 originated in the United States and spread to capitalist countries throughout Europe, it has formed an intensification of the economic panic in capitalist countries around the world. Under these circumstances, the only way for capitalist countries to preserve their last breath is to encourage exports and restrict imports. Under the latter policy is the construction of high tariff barriers to resist the import of foreign goods. This is the so-called peaceful tariff war. And under the former policy is the intensified exploitation of weak nations and colonies, making them more impoverished, while further extracting their cheap raw materials, and even further planning to re-divide the world.

Domestic Goods Forum

Work That Should Be Done in the Domestic Goods Year

— Pan Yangjie

In order to cultivate the faith and determination of Chinese people in domestic goods, the 22nd year of the Republic of China has been designated as the Year of Domestic Goods. Since the opening ceremony of this year's New Year's Day, these 365 days have been carrying a major mission at all times and must be completed without any slackness. Under the heavy national difficulties of politics and economy, being able to engage in practical work of avenging humiliation and resisting foreign aggression, the Year of Domestic Goods is indeed a very meaningful and valuable thing; however, there can only be a harvest after cultivation. We must realize all slogans and ideals before the ideal success can be achieved. Therefore, when the Year of Domestic Goods begins, we must not regard the propaganda of the opening ceremony as the completion of the work. After the opening ceremony, we must shoulder this arduous responsibility, cherish every second, and embark on the road to future success through hard work. Only by completing the work that should be done in the Year of Domestic Goods can we live up to the New Year's Day opening ceremony that contains great significance, and only then will we not waste the Year of Domestic Goods that bears a major mission!

How exactly can we cultivate the faith and determination of Chinese people in domestic goods? Analyzing the current national crisis can indeed move the emotions of the general public. However, according to the theory of marketing, the foreign goods that emphasize huge advertising costs and extremely strong sales power always threaten our emerging industries; and the facts further tell us that in the Chinese market flooded with foreign goods, to establish faith in domestic goods, in addition to advocating the use of domestic goods, there must be cooperation in production and sales to achieve victory on both the offensive and defensive sides of the commercial war. In the Year of Domestic Goods, we naturally cannot avoid working hard on this important task for the sake of resisting foreign aggression, avenging humiliation, and establishing faith in domestic goods; however, transportation, sales, and production are complex problems in themselves. If we do not have a scientific design in this short year, we will often delay due to paying attention to one thing and losing sight of another. Therefore, in order to accelerate and focus, it is best to take the month as a unit during the Year of Domestic Goods and hold a specific movement every month. Regarding production and sales aspects, such as improvements in production, coordination of labor and management, attention to personnel, financial turnover, etc., are originally specialized problems that cannot be solved in a short period of time, but they are also basic work in the Year of Domestic Goods movement and cannot be abandoned because of their complexity. If we designate one month to specialize in research, discussion, and experimentation, we should be able to obtain practical results. Therefore, we hope that the twelve months of the Year of Domestic Goods will all bear a mission and will not be wasted. According to the need and order, we will separately study (1) improvement of production; (2) efforts in sales; (3) removal of transportation difficulties; (4) financial turnover; (5) factory standardization; (6) raw material issues; (7) cost reduction issues; (8) how to cater to the customs of people in various regions; (9) training of salespeople; (10) labor issues; (11) cooperation between production, sales, and consumption; (12) implementation of consumer cooperation; from all aspects of domestic goods production and sales, we will seek fundamental improvements, establish standardization of domestic goods, consolidate the people's faith in domestic goods, and fulfill the meaning and mission of the Year of Domestic Goods.

The regional target of the Year of Domestic Goods is not limited to one place, and Shanghai is only the target of this movement. However, in this abnormal situation where foreign goods have penetrated into the inland areas, if the domestic goods movement does not expand from one place to various places, from cities to villages, the vast market will still not be able to be taken back from the hands of foreign goods. Therefore, after the specific implementation of the domestic goods movement in Shanghai, we should go to the inland areas to establish the faith of the national public in domestic goods and encourage the national public to make the determination to use domestic goods. However, the domestic goods movement in the inland areas does not need to use text or verbal propaganda exclusively. The domestic goods exhibitions held in Guangzhou, Qingdao, Henan, Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Suzhou, and other places recently have introduced our original and newly created domestic goods to the general public, which has a great effect. Education institutions and industrial groups in various places can follow suit. As for the original special products in various places, after exhibitions and promotion, further improvements are made in terms of production. At a time when the rural economy is on the verge of danger, many people who have difficulties in life have been able to resolve them by advocating sideline occupations.

In the Year of Domestic Goods, in addition to carrying out practical movements in small units every month and promoting the domestic goods movement to various places, we should set up more domestic goods introduction agencies in various places to make consumers aware of domestic goods and introduce emerging domestic products to various places. Recently, the Shanghai China National Products Production and Sales Cooperation Association, the China National Products Guidance Center, and the Chongqing National Products Introduction Center have been striving to carry out this mission with good results. The industrial circles in Qingdao and Shantou have also seen this and have already started preparations. If we can start from the above-mentioned domestic goods introduction agencies that have already been established and have achieved results, and gradually expand, it will be of great help to this enthusiastic domestic goods movement!

The Future of Our Country's Textile Industry (Middle) Zhu Xianhang

—

(A) Rationalize operations ... Don't engage in speculation ... Seek simplicity in exports ... Demand that raw cotton consistently meet standards (B) Rationalize work ... Reduce expenses (C) The government vigorously implements protective policies (D) The financial community regards large-scale textile investment as powerful cooperation (E) Chinese people purchase and use domestically produced textiles

B. Rationalization of Work

Industrial rationalization is the general term for standardization, simplification, and scientific management. It originated in Germany after the European War and was used to revive the collapsing industry. All countries have followed suit and promoted it to the fullest extent. As an industrially backward country, we should urgently take action to implement it. Moreover, with foreign cotton goods dumping in our country, our textile industry is fundamentally at risk of being shaken. There is no way to reverse the decline without actively implementing it. The so-called standardization, simplification, and scientific management refer to both machinery and work. The mechanical part has been described in detail in my book "Methods for Rationalizing Textile Work." The main point is to simplify the project, improve efficiency, and increase production to reduce costs. In terms of the rationalization of work, the only way is to reduce expenses, maximize the potential of workers, reduce the number of people, and improve their wages, so that individual income can be increased, while the total number of workers is reduced. Expenses include interest, wages, materials, salary for those with power, and miscellaneous expenses. The number of wages is the largest and the most flexible. The same work can be done by several people or by one person. When several people do one job, the total income is always more than the income of one person doing the same job because it is necessary to maintain the lives of several people. If the income is less, it is always difficult to make a living. Why not maximize their potential, reduce the number of people, and improve their wages to reduce the total amount of wages and reduce expenses? As for power materials, they must also follow the progress of technology, simplify the project, and seek to reduce their quantity. If expenses are reduced, the cost will be lower. Even if it is sold at a low price, it can be sold smoothly and will not suffer losses. For example, if the cost can be reduced by one or two, I can get one or two of profit when others sell at the original price, and I can avoid losses when others lose one or two. If our textile industry can work to rationalize, what is there to worry about dumping their yarn cloth.

Industrial Tidbits

— Mie Ran

Yesterday, I visited Mr. Wu Yun-chu, a chemical industrialist who had returned from a study tour of Europe and the United States. What he said was quite helpful for readers.

Mr. Wu's study tour lasted for more than five months. His footsteps were all over Europe, America, Japan, and the Nanyang countries. He spent 20,000 yuan and gained a lot. It is said that he was tireless during his study tour, writing reports, recording his experiences, and writing letters at night. Sometimes he went to the library to study, and sometimes he went to the laboratory to experiment. He was diligent and happy, and he was admirable. Mr. Wu said: He will soon expand two factories, hoping to make a great contribution to the national chemical industry.

Mr. Wu said that the depression in European and American industries has reached its extreme. Workers only work five days a week, and only five hours a day, and there are countless unemployed. This is partly due to the sharp decline in purchasing power around the world, and partly due to the rapid progress of scientific management. Small factories that use manual labor and semi-mechanical methods have no place to stand.

Wu Yan said that the use of omnipotent machines and the progress of scientific management have made the world's artificial labor useless. Machines are becoming more sophisticated every day, and human resources are being eliminated every day. Mr. Wu visited a large carbon gas factory, which was very large in scale and was powered by machines, but there were only three employees.

Editor's Note

My friend Mr. Lu Xin returned from Japan after studying crafts. When he talked about the Japanese running industry, he always used his full spirit, buried his head and did it to death. After any difficulties, he refused to give up. There is a pencil maker who has a history of thirty years. His hair is already gray, and his son has graduated from university. He also helps him work, without getting tired, without being respectful, without taking shortcuts, without being greedy for small profits, and without seeking quick success. Therefore, he can produce excellent products, lower costs, and make daily progress. Mr. Lu couldn't help but feel admiration. Japan is indeed my enemy, but its spirit and perseverance in running industry cannot be said to be not my teacher.

The sound of Shanhaiguan, when we try to close our eyes, we should recall the tragic situation of Zhabei on January 28th. When the country is in danger, our national goods factories should be prepared to serve the country. It is said that Japan had factories that manufactured commodities converted into military supplies during wartime, such as can factories converting into bombs, cotton weaving factories converting into military uniforms, enamel steel factories converting into iron hats and kettles, etc. A friend who returned from Japan had a plan for each factory to convert into military supplies, which made people shudder after reading it. Being the same people, living in the same country, when the country is in such a crisis, now is the time for industrialists to serve the country.

"There are still many good foreign goods that domestic goods don't have. Factory owners should quickly think of alternatives to domestic goods."

Everyone can say this ready-made sentence. But the prerequisite for running a domestic goods factory is economy and talent. Under the current situation, if domestic goods manufacturers do not have working capital, will financiers be sincerely and truly assisting them? If domestic goods manufacturers do not have real talents, will education institutions be able to humbly and diligently cultivate young people to meet the needs of factories? If there is no sincerity and strength, no matter how good you say it, it will not help at all, so please don't say it.

Since Chongqing organized the Domestic Goods Introduction Center, everyone has hoped that all localities will follow suit. Sure enough, recently, Mr. Li Zumo came from Qingdao and said that he had organized a Shandong Domestic Goods Introduction Center. Mr. Shi Menghu came from Shantou and said that he would organize a Shantou Domestic Goods Introduction Center. Lei Weinan, Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Guangxi, also said that he would organize a Guangxi Domestic Goods Introduction Center after returning to Guangxi. These surging domestic goods introduction centers are all being established in this Year of Domestic Goods, which is very gratifying. On the Shanghai side, there is the China National Products Company, which is about to open. This news is of great help to the promotion of domestic goods. I hope that all localities will actively carry out these things, and contact each other. I think that places like Hankou, Tianjin, Guangzhou, Fuzhou, Zhengzhou, and Taiyuan all have the potential to set up domestic goods introduction centers. At the same time, our manufacturers in Shanghai should organize domestic goods tour groups to visit and inspect various places in person, so as to further contact each other, so that we will not live up to this Year of Domestic Goods.

This issue has received many contributions from various places, most of which are very valuable, but due to the limited space, we have to publish them one after another. I hope everyone will understand!

Discussion on Promoting Domestic Goods

— Cao Yimin

Mr. Cao studied scientific management and sales in the United States and is currently the personnel section chief of Sanyou Industrial Company. This article is based on his experience and is very valuable. (Editor)

The 22nd year of the Republic of China is designated as the Year of Domestic Goods, so during this year; whether individuals, families, or groups purchase items, they must first choose from domestic products. However, what is domestic product? What is imported product? It is difficult to distinguish. Although the name is a domestic goods store, there are inevitably still imported products mixed in; in order to seek profit, there are often goods appearing on the market that have been changed. Buyers buy them back as domestic goods, and later it is confirmed by others that they are imported products; therefore, they must be very annoyed, and even discouraged from buying domestic goods again. This really disappoints the enthusiasm of those who love to use domestic goods in general. I myself have also encountered the above facts. In my personal opinion; it is best to ask the chamber of commerce to set up a commodity exhibition hall in a bustling area, not only displaying domestic products, but also displaying imported products. Domestic goods and imported products are displayed in one cabinet, with analysis and identification. Under the observation of the masses, they can know which is superior and which is inferior; patriotic people will be happy to purchase and use domestic goods, and at the same time can increase the public's knowledge of identifying domestic products. And I hope that major companies will also adopt this kind of identification display method, this is just a little bit of my humble opinion. Another point is about the employees in the domestic goods market; the staff in the domestic goods market must understand the importance of their responsibility. The salesmen in the domestic goods market are pioneers who have the ideology of seeking survival for the country and striving for glory for the nation. His merit is equal to that of the soldiers on the front line; therefore, this kind of staff must absolutely sacrifice their personal, courageous service spirit, then they must be aggressive in their daily work, and be able to treat customers considerately and diligently, and make buyers satisfied, so that buyers will be happy to buy domestic goods again next time; so as not to be like the shop assistants in ordinary stores who always drive away customers, so that buyers will have the bad feeling that they will not want to visit again after one transaction. I hope that the leaders who manage the domestic goods company will pay close attention to this issue.

Jiangsu Education Funds to Continue Distribution

Estimated Expenditure for January

Jiangsu provincial schools and social education institutions' expenses for September (November for Zou teachers and Shixiao), the fund disbursement notices, although filled and issued by the Education Fund Management Office, and the date of written collection of funds was January 15th, it is heard that the Education Fund Management Office, in order to actively raise these funds, first sent Section Chief Liu Beihe to Wuxian, Wujiang and other places to borrow funds, Wuxian borrowed 20,000, Wujiang borrowed 10,000, Liu Beihe returned to the office at the end of December, and Section Chief Liu Zishen went to Songjiang to borrow funds, returned to the office on January 6th, and also borrowed 20,000. The Management Office heard on January 10th that the budget audit committee decided to allocate half a month's funds to the county for the November disbursement notice, and the remaining half month would still be paid in cash. The disbursement notice has been partially filled in the office, and the audit committee will sign again on the 12th. Senior High School Curriculum Standards (6)

(17) Occasionally use games, competitions, and performances to review old materials, so as to increase interest and practice application.

(18) Oral practice should not only focus on the correctness of each part, but also on the fluency of the whole part, so as to conform to the nature of language. (19) In the practice of listening and pronunciation, use as much visual aid as possible, such as recognizing and looking at phonetic symbols, observing the position of pronunciation, etc., so that students can easily grasp it.

(20) Pay attention to the combined changes of phonemes that should be in words and sentences, such as assimilation and connection, so as to conform to the situation of living language.

(21) Reading work should focus on silent reading and supplement with loud reading, so as to suit the usual purposes and easily increase the speed and interest of reading.

(22) The materials for extracurricular browsing should first be derived from the materials familiarized in the class, so that extracurricular reading has a considerable motive.

(23) In browsing-style reading, special attention must be paid to the analysis of meaning, and not to be stagnant on unimportant new words, so that reading is fast and smooth and meets the needs of life.

(24) In browsing-style reading, the timing method must be used frequently to practice large speed, so as to develop the habit of rapid reading.

(25) Pay attention to the calligraphy in all writing works, and encourage students to write neatly and beautifully, so that they can have considerable progress. (26) All compositions must pay attention to the clarity of ideas and the simplicity, accuracy and common use of writing, so as to avoid random writing and create all kinds of strange English that are not applicable in content and appearance.

(27) Preliminary composition must first prepare the meaning of the content and the necessary vocabulary from the oral aspect, so as to reduce errors and develop the habit of preparing adequately before writing.

(28) The length of free composition must be based on very short ones as a principle, so as to avoid being more and not being refined, and on the contrary, develop the habit of making mistakes often.

(29) All errors in composition, wherever students can correct themselves, they must be guided to correct themselves, so as to develop the habit of prudence. (30) Systematized grammar must first start from the relevant key points of the materials that have been learned or are being learned, and then collect examples of what has been learned and what has not been learned, and extend to related key points. After that, the systematized parts must be applied frequently to solve grammatical difficulties in various works, so as to fully obtain the benefits of induction and deduction.

(31) The scope of grammar systematization must be gradually expanded according to the procedure, and must not be hasty, so as to suit the level and obtain real benefits.

(32) Grammar teaching must pay special attention to the differences between English and Chinese, so that it is easy to learn relatively pure English and perceive the characteristics of the structure of the two languages.

(33) Fully express the commonness of rhetorical principles, so that students can use the essentials learned in English to languages other than English.

(34) Grammar and rhetoric essentials, after students have understood, then add supplementary exercises as needed to make it easy to apply.

History

First, Objectives

(1) To narrate the expansion of our nation, and the changes in culture, politics, and society through the dynasties, in order to explain the origin of the current state of our country, and to jointly promote the historical basis of the Three Principles of the People.

(2) To focus on the course of modern diplomatic failures and the origin of political and economic problems in order to explain the background of the national revolution in our country, and to indicate the efforts that the nation should make in the future.

(3) Past political and economic issues that have an impact on modern society should be given special attention, so that students can gain insights from historical facts to study modern concerns and cultivate their ability to observe and judge. (4) To narrate the development of various important nations, and the changes in culture, politics, and society of various countries, so that students can gain a correct understanding of the trends of world currents.

(5) To explain the development of modern imperialism, the general trend of national movements, and the origin of important modern international issues, in order to study our country's countermeasures to world events, and to promote the realization of freedom and equality internationally.

(6) To narrate the contributions of various nations to world culture, and the state of their academic thought evolution. Special attention should be paid to the impact of science on modern civilization, in order to promote the efforts of our nation to catch up in culture.

Appendix: The objectives listed on the right are to continue the objectives of the junior high school history curriculum standards, with special attention to the following points.

Registration of Primary School Teachers Organized by the Municipal Bureau of Education

Registration from January 16th to 21st

Physical examination and oral test on the 23rd and 24th

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued a notice yesterday regarding the seventh registration of primary school teachers. The notice stated that the bureau has been conducting primary school teacher registration to carefully select primary school teachers. Now that the semester is about to change, the seventh primary school teacher registration will be held. Registration will begin at 9:00 am on January 16th and close at 1:00 pm on January 21st. Physical examinations and oral tests will be held at the bureau on January 23rd and 24th. Those who wish to serve as primary school teachers in this city and have the qualifications stipulated in the primary school teacher registration regulations should register and take the examination at the bureau on time. The registration regulations and registration instructions can be obtained from the bureau. For the convenience of readers, the registration regulations and registration instructions are appended below.

▲Registration Regulations Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education Primary School Teacher Registration Regulations, Article 1: Primary school teachers in this city shall register with the Bureau in accordance with these regulations. Article 2: Those who have obtained one of the following qualifications in national, provincial, municipal, county, and registered private schools, and who pass the oral test and physical examination, shall be allowed to register: 1. Graduates of university education departments, education colleges, or normal universities; 2. Graduates of university undergraduate (excluding education departments), higher normal schools, or advanced normal specialized courses; 3. Graduates of specialized schools (excluding higher normal schools); 4. Graduates of senior high school normal departments or normal undergraduate courses; 5. Graduates of rural normal schools with a study period of four years or more; 6. Graduates of senior high schools or old-system middle schools, but this does not apply to those who have worked in non-educational institutions for more than two years after graduation; 7. Graduates of vocational schools (equivalent to senior high schools) or old-system Class A vocational schools, but this does not apply to those who have worked in institutions unrelated to their specialized subjects for more than two years after graduation; 8. Graduates of rural normal schools or normal training courses with a study period of three years or less and two years or more, but this does not apply to those who have worked in non-educational institutions for more than two years after graduation; 9. Graduates of nanny training schools or nanny courses with a study period of two years or more, but this does not apply to those who have worked in non-educational institutions for more than two years after graduation. Article 3: Those who have passed the certification and have not exceeded the prescribed time limit shall be allowed to register, and the effective time of registration shall be the same as the effective time of certification. Article 4: Teachers who are allowed to register and meet the qualifications of the first, second, fourth, fifth, sixth, and eighth items of the preceding article shall be allowed to serve as homeroom teachers. Those who meet the qualifications of the third and seventh items shall be allowed to serve as specialized teachers. Those who meet the qualifications of the ninth item shall be allowed to serve as nannies. Those who meet the qualifications of the third item shall be allowed to serve in the certified teaching position. Article 5: Teachers who have been approved for registration and continue to work in non-educational institutions or institutions unrelated to their specialized subjects for more than two years, their registration shall be invalid. Article 6: When registering, two primary school teacher registration forms must be filled out, with a recent 2.5-inch half-length photo attached. Article 7: When registering, the graduation certificate, study certificate, certification certificate, service certificate, etc. shall be submitted for verification and returned after the registration is announced. Article 8: Those who are allowed to register will be issued a registration form, and those who fail will not be issued a registration form. Article 9: The registration date for each session shall be announced by the Bureau in the newspaper. Article 10: These regulations may be amended at any time if there are any matters not covered. Article 11: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Municipal Government.

Natural Power

Electricity: China 5, China is still in its infancy, while hundreds of thousands of progressive people use electricity everywhere.

Land Power: China 30, Agriculture is immature, and mineral resources are undeveloped, while hundreds of thousands improve agriculture and develop mineral resources extensively.

Solar Power: China 50, A majority of the land is still barren, while hundreds of thousands can turn barren land into fertile land.

Hydropower: China 20, Without scientific methods, the gains are minimal, while hundreds of thousands use scientific methods for shipping, power generation, irrigation, and cultivation.

Atmospheric Power: China 1, Apart from breathing, there is no other use, while hundreds of thousands transform all things and engage in extensive manufacturing.

Collective Power: China 30, There is unity but little organization, and the organization is extremely incomplete, while hundreds of thousands unite with more organization, and the organization is extremely complete.

Brain Power: China 20, Education is not widespread, and 90% of the people do not use their brains, while hundreds of thousands popularize education, and 90% of the people use their brains.

Physical Strength: China 100, Entirely relying on physical strength for work, resulting in labor and poverty, while hundreds of thousands use human bodies to command machines for work, resulting in ease and wealth.

Mechanical Power: China 1, China is uniquely in its infancy, while hundreds of thousands are good at using mechanical power to replace physical strength.

Time Power: China 100, Not valuing time and wasting time, while hundreds of thousands value time and save time.

China Foreign Country Comparison of Chinese and Foreign Goods and Quantities

Most of the foreign imports are manufactured goods and a small portion of agricultural products, all created using brain power, mechanical power, collective power, and minimal physical strength, and are of high quality. In recent years, the exchange rate has risen sharply, resulting in even greater losses for China.

Most of the Chinese exports are agricultural products, almost entirely created using physical strength, and are of low quality. Although the exchange rate is high, the gains are very limited.

Registration Instructions

Shanghai Primary School Teacher Registration Instructions, 1. All those who wish to apply for positions as teachers in municipal or registered private primary schools in this city and have not registered shall register with the Bureau in accordance with the "Registration Regulations." 2. Those who meet one of the qualification requirements stipulated in Article 2 of the "Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education Primary School Teacher Registration Regulations" and have complete procedures shall be allowed to register. 3. When registering, two registration forms must be filled out in person, with a recent 2.5-inch half-length photo attached, along with the graduation certificate, study certificate, certification certificate, service certificate, etc., all submitted to the registration office, and a temporary receipt will be given. The registration documents will be returned later upon presentation of the receipt, but the certificates must be kept for verification and will not be returned. 4. If the photos on the graduation certificate or certificate are missing, they must be completely supplemented. 5. If the graduation year has exceeded two years, a recent service certificate must be attached. 6. Registration forms that are not completely filled out or have incomplete procedures will not be accepted. 7. Graduation certificates from private schools that have not been verified as registered or have not been stamped by the competent authority shall be deemed invalid. 8. The submitted registration documents shall be returned upon presentation of the original receipt after the end of this registration period and shall not be withdrawn in the middle. 9. Those who should not take the oral test or physical examination will not be registered. 10. All registered personnel must take back the registration documents with the original receipt within one month after the announcement in the newspaper.

The Municipal Bureau of Education Urges All Schools to Submit Teaching Timetables

And graduation certificates, student status investigation forms, etc. The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education instructed all municipal and private registered primary and secondary schools yesterday, stating that the teaching timetable, student graduation certificates, and student status investigation forms for new and transfer students, which should be submitted to the Bureau for approval each semester, should be submitted to the Bureau within a certain period of time, as previously ordered. However, due to long-term negligence, many schools can report within the prescribed time limit, while others delay and postpone reporting, which seriously hinders the progress of public affairs. Therefore, the previous order is reiterated, and all primary and secondary schools are ordered that the teaching timetable should be submitted to the Bureau within two weeks after the start of the semester, and the student graduation certificates and student status investigation forms for new and transfer students should be submitted to the Bureau within one month. Other documents that should be submitted to the Bureau for approval shall be submitted as soon as possible in accordance with the specified period and shall not be delayed. This is imperative.
