The American Source Research Society has published the entire Encyclopedia Source Series, totaling ten giant volumes. In addition to covering various subjects, the content also focuses on research and exploration. It is said that after purchasing the books, there are special rights. For ten years, if you want to investigate business conditions and various academic issues, you can inquire by letter at any time, and you will receive a detailed answer in the shortest possible time. The society employs hundreds of experts who are responsible for answering questions. In addition, every six months, the society gathers and sends valuable questions and answers and fresh information from various places, so that in addition to the ten giant volumes, there are annual additions. The society aims to stimulate research interest, and it is very suitable for schools, businesses, libraries, etc. to purchase, especially for children and students who study at home, it is better than hiring experts and professors in various subjects. Moved to Baseball Field

丨Nothing more than to sell tickets丨

Two matches rescheduled - Donghua vs. French Business - Youyou vs. Western Police

The Scotia Cup final between Argyll and Lancashire, which was scheduled to be held at the Racecourse this Saturday, as previously reported, has been announced by the secretariat of the Western Football Association that the executive committee of the Western Football Association held a meeting on Tuesday evening to discuss the Argyll vs. Lancashire Scotia Cup final, which will attract many spectators. If it is held at the Racecourse, Chinese spectators will lose the opportunity to watch this important match. For this reason, the two Group A matches originally scheduled for this Saturday at the Chinese Baseball Field and the Chinese Football Field, Donghua vs. French Business and Youyou vs. Western Police, have been postponed, and the Argyll vs. Lancashire Scotia Cup final has been moved to the Chinese Baseball Field and will also be a charity match. Tickets are divided into two types: 40 cents and one yuan. (Note: The use of this charity match has not yet been specified.) Western Youth Women's Basketball Association Concludes Liangjiang Wins Green Team Retains Championship

28丨32 Liangjiang Turns Defeat into Victory after a Crushing First Half

Chen Rongming's Amazing Performance Dominates the Entire Court

Southeast Team Runner-Up

The Liangjiang Women's Basketball Team retained the Western Youth Women's Basketball Association championship for the second year in a row. In the final match last night, they defeated their strong opponent, the Rowing Green Team, with a score of 30 to 28, creating a perfect record of nine wins in nine games. The runner-up Southeast Team defeated the Blue Team yesterday. The Blue Team was deemed to have forfeited due to using an unregistered player. There were also two other matches: Liangjiang B lost to the Yellow Team, and Chongde forfeited to the Red Team. The current Western Youth Women's Basketball Tournament has ended in its entirety (except for one non-championship match between the Blue Team and the Yellow Team) and is declared closed.

▲Liangjiang Team Escapes Death

Chen Rongming Supports the World Single-Handedly

Liangjiang's ability to defeat their strong opponent, turn defeat into victory, and the great credit goes to center Chen Rongming, whose agility, stability, and speed of movement are rarely seen. The shots from the left and right along the sidelines into the basket are truly a sight to behold. Chen Rongming scored 24 points out of Liangjiang's 32 points, which is truly not easy. Although Pan Meng did not score, her assistance was significant and she was able to run back and forth. Yang Sen did not show her strengths. Among the guards, Huang Shuhua was sharp throughout the entire court and stood out, intercepting countless balls. Chen Baixue and Shi Ruixia did their best and did not diminish in color due to their small size, and their performance was very satisfying.

Green Team Unleashes Fierce Attack in the First Half

In the first half, Liangjiang was in a losing situation, and everyone on the court was worried. Although Chen Rongming scored the first point with a free throw, the Green Team relied on its tall stature and passed the ball two or three times to reach the basket, scoring with a shot. The forwards were also very difficult to get the ball. The Green Team's strong players Fei Labiling Lu and others scored again and again, scoring six consecutive goals. The Green Team had 12 points, while Liangjiang had only one point. After Chen Rongming's struggle, the first quarter ended with a crushing defeat of 14 to 6.

Gradually Catching Up, the Situation Gradually Changes

The second quarter was the turning point for Liangjiang. Pan Meng replaced Chen Jucai and focused on attacking from both sides, which proved successful. The Green Team scored two more points, and Yang Sen also followed suit, scoring into the net. Chen Rongming continued, and Yang Sen scored two more consecutive goals, adding eight points. At the end of the first half, Liangjiang was only two points behind with 14 to 16.

Liangjiang Finds an Opportunity and Jumps to the Top

In the second half, Liangjiang went from a crushing defeat to catching up, then surpassing and jumping to the top. At this point, the Green Team's entire lineup wavered, missing shots and panicking. Chen Rongming turned around and rushed into the basket, scoring three consecutive goals, and surpassed the Green Team with 20 to 10. It then became 24 to 18. At the end of the third quarter, it was 24 to 22. In the final match, Chen Rongming succeeded again, winning by eight points with a maximum score of 32 to 24. The final score was 32 to 28. The referees were Ms. Kemmer and Shu Hong.

Fifth Western Youth Volleyball Tournament

Registration Closes on the 20th

The official start of the competition on the 28th

Invitation letters have been sent, but other teams will be accepted at discretion.

The Fifth Annual Volleyball Tournament of the Western Youth Association is underway. Invitation letters to participate have been sent to various teams, such as the Mike Ling Team, Western Youth Team, Chinese Youth Team, etc. The Chinese Youth Team has won the championship of the association for three consecutive years. According to the Western Youth Sports Department, other teams that have not received invitation letters and wish to participate can register and will be accepted at discretion. According to this year's plan, the competition will be divided into Group A and Group B, with Group A being stronger and Group B being weaker. Business News

Spot Gold Floods Market, Gold Price Plummets Nine Taels

Swap Deals Nearly Exhausted

Source of Supply Unimpeded, No Major Impact

(Central Bank Repeatedly Sells Spot, Unable to Curb Decline) Yesterday's market for standard gold bars was no less chaotic than the previous day. The pessimism reached its peak. Initially, large bars fell by 0.0625, American Bank fell by 0.125, and exchange rates all rose. Forward silver prices suddenly increased by more than 1%. Bank private telegraphs also increased by 0.125 accordingly. Therefore, the opening price was low at 798.5 taels. The exchange market opened with the near-term British exchange rate at 1 shilling, 7 pence, and 0.0625, and the American dollar at 28.0625 yuan, also stronger than the previous closing. After opening, the market immediately went downstream. Subsequently, due to banks' willingness to take delivery, the market also improved and rebounded, reaching 99 taels and 7 mace, but failed to break through the 800 tael mark. Although the Central Bank opened spot tenders, the large arrival of spot goods undermined confidence, despite the near exhaustion of swap deals. HSBC quoted British long at 0.125, while American rose by 0.25, seemingly excessive. The gold and exchange markets turned sluggish, and the decline was extremely severe, mainly due to a lack of buyers. At 92.5 taels, the Central Bank continued to inject spot, and the Hengxing, Qianchangxiang, Dadecheng, Tongfengheng, and other agents bought for term bidding, providing support. A Review of the Silver Market Over the Past Year

Decline in Silver Production Does Not Benefit Silver Prices

The Reason Lies in the Slump of Sino-Indian Commerce

▲Restoring Sino-British Purchasing Power Can Restore Silver Prices▲

The most important influence on the silver market last year was the absolute reduction in the demand for silver in the East. Seventy-five percent of the world's silver production is usually absorbed by China and India. In 1929, which had the largest silver production of 261.61 million taels, the two countries absorbed nearly 84 percent. Although silver production decreased to 160.6 million taels last year, China and India consumed only 52 million taels, accounting for only 32 percent of the production.

Hunter and Harman said that if China and India were to become silver-selling countries, there is no doubt that world silver would constantly stand below the lowest record in world silver. Today, China and India are the world's largest silver-using countries. Normally, at this lowest record in silver history, they have reduced their purchasing power. There must be a reason for this. In our experience, the reason is not the reduction in silver prices, but the reduction in world purchases of Chinese and Indian export goods.

Analyzing the reason for the slump in the silver market, the consensus is that the silver currency system is not working. But the real reason is that the East must increase its purchasing power. To increase purchasing power, the goods of China and India must be sold smoothly in the world market. Therefore, if the commerce of the two countries can be revived and prices increase, it will be of great benefit to the silver market.

Hender and Harman have no derogative intention regarding speculation, because speculation is indeed an essential aspect of regulating the market. However, they consider it unwise for speculators to raise silver prices last year, because the silver market has never had a stable reason to provide speculators with information.

According to their estimates, the silver production in 1932 was approximately 160.6 million taels (160,600,000), of which the United States produced 23.4 million taels (31,400,000), Mexico 71.7 million taels (88,900,000), Canada 18.3 million taels (20,400,000), South Africa 12.4 million taels (19,700,000), and other parts of the world 34.8 million taels (35,700,000).

The supply of old silver in 1932 is estimated to be approximately 22.6 million taels, of which the Indian government sold 24 million taels (35,000,000). The total of new and old silver is 270.2 million taels.

It is estimated that of the 270.2 million taels of silver consumed in 1932, India consumed 12 million taels, China (including Hong Kong) 40 million taels, and Germany 22.8 million taels.

The amount of silver used for industrial and decorative purposes in the United States and Canada is approximately 22 million taels, in the United Kingdom approximately 8 million taels, and in Mexico approximately 1 million taels. The amount used for silver coins is estimated to be 20 million taels in Germany, 23.2 million taels in Mexico, 2.8 million taels in Cuba, 500,000 taels in Yugoslavia, and the remaining 1.2 million taels are stored in the United States. The other 53.7 million taels are scattered throughout the world.

London futures: March, May, and August each down 25. The Java white kernel market remains unchanged.

Metal: American Huisi Iron Received Telegram Yesterday Regarding Spot Goods

American Huisi iron. Overseas factories have long reported a shortage of goods. Although traders in this port who want to place orders have been inquiring everywhere, the foreign firms' replies consistently state that the factories have no goods. Yesterday, American companies such as Shen Chang, Hua Da, and Mei Kang received telegrams from factories in New York stating that there were over 400 tons of spot goods available, priced at US$5.70 per case (200 pounds) (equivalent to 25 taels in Shanghai, including miscellaneous expenses). Therefore, traders in this port felt that the price was too high and difficult to calculate, so they countered with a price of US$5.45. However, whether the transaction can be completed will depend on the telegram from the foreign firms tomorrow. It is reported that the shipment period is in February and March.

Spring and Autumn

Dark Arcadia

— Zhan Lu

The Shanxi Model Province, an Arcadia that people yearn for, has received unanimous praise from observers from all sides in the more than ten years since the establishment of the Republic of China. In the last six or seven years, this praise has become nothing! What is particularly despairing is reading the Taiyuan dispatch on the suppression of opium in Shanxi Province published in this newspaper! Unexpectedly, the Arcadia would be so dark.

The dispatch says that Shanxi, which has turned into a (illegible), has recently been flooded with drugs; in the counties of the central route, the sales of white (illegible) (i.e., heroin) are worth more than 300,000 taels annually, with each tael worth 60-70 silver dollars. In the southern route area, red pills (i.e., gold pills) are selling well everywhere. These few reports are enough to show that the homes of the Arcadia have been shrouded in layers of dark clouds of poison, not to mention the dark situation in Shanxi Province is more than this?

Tao Yuanming's masterpiece! Peach Blossom Spring is about obtaining great light from small light. The record says "It seemed as if there was light," which is called small light. "Walking a few dozen steps further, it suddenly opened up," which is called great light. When it comes to Shanxi Province, which is known as Arcadia, it is about obtaining great darkness from small light. Since the establishment of the Republic of China, wars have broken out frequently in various provinces, but only this Arcadia has been relatively peaceful, which is called small light. Until now, Arcadia is flooded with drugs; it is not good to say "Walking a few dozen steps further, it suddenly opened up," it only deserves to be said that after twenty years, it is mistakenly dark. The happiness of the people in Peach Blossom Spring can only be seen in Mr. Tao's record! "The elderly and children were all happily enjoying themselves," which is truly a "Utopian scene of happiness." The current Arcadia can also be called Utopia, but it should be interpreted differently, as a place where opium is entrusted! As for "The elderly and children were all happily enjoying themselves," these two sentences are no longer applicable, what is applicable is gold pills and white powder, and they are openly sold.

Arcadia has changed into anti-Arcadia, and then into dark Arcadia. Whose fault is this?

Implicit Praise and Criticism

— Xu Jie

The same old tricks of the second master!

In the final years of the Zhou Dynasty, when the feudal lords were rebellious and the world was obviously in great chaos, that old Mr. Confucius of Qufu simply had no way to solve it. Although he served as prime minister in the State of Lu for four months, he was unable to develop his ambitions. He had no choice but to travel around the various states, hoping to meet like-minded people to take action. Coincidentally, at this time, all the states wanted to become hegemons and champions, and their minds were full of swords and spears, tricky and eccentric ideas. Who would listen to your benevolence and righteousness? Mr. Confucius had no choice but to return to his hometown dejectedly, picked up his pen, and wrote a "Spring and Autumn Annals." Originally, the writing style of the Spring and Autumn Annals was very cautious, with the purpose of implicitly praising and criticizing the figures of the time, so as to deter rebellious and treacherous subjects. Although his proud disciples, such as Ziyou and Zixia, could not praise a single word, it can be seen how cautious Mr. Confucius was. However, although Mr. Confucius wrote this great article, by the Warring States period, the world became even more chaotic and out of control. Although Mencius emerged and advised people not to value the word "profit," it was of no use. As a result, everyone slaughtered each other, and after more than two hundred years, the Han Dynasty finally brought peace. Although Mr. Confucius's great work "Spring and Autumn Annals" was ignored by everyone at the time, who dares to say that it has no value now? The current China is like the closing of the Spring and Autumn period and the opening of the Warring States period. Mr. Lin Yutang is rushing to write a "Analects," and Mr. Zhou Shoujuan is also rushing to write a "Spring and Autumn Annals," both wanting to play the old tricks of the second master Confucius. Their ambitions are commendable, but in fact, they are of no use at all! I'm not just talking nonsense, isn't everyone still playing with Sun Tzu's Art of War and the Yellow Stone Duke's Six Secret Teachings? Otherwise, it's better to write a few books like Guiguzi, Tao Te Ching, and Zhuangzi. I don't know what the two gentlemen think?

A Perspective on the Metropolis

— Long Sao

丨The Line of Life Between Two Classes丨

Giant cranes are hoisted high in mid-air, holding iron bars and wood stones, digging deep into the strata, erecting magnificent and exquisite buildings or residences. As you walk along Great West Road, Avenue Road, Route Massenet, Museum Road, Nanjing Road, North Sichuan Road, etc., you will see these buildings that are exchanged for tens of millions of gold. There, there are hot water radiators that drive away the cold of winter, there are high-class elevators that replace people's walking, there are elegantly decorated gardens, there are plump Nordic breeds of dogs, there are proud servants, and there is the scent of perfume...

A 1934-style car is parked on the side of the door, a Russian strongman holding a pistol standing next to the master or mistress,

young masters and young ladies sitting around the fireplace talking about movie stars and the like. Shanghai, this Shanghai of the rich, is as beautiful as spring flowers, as bright as gold, and as fragrant as wine!

A gentleman, along with his family, chain-like servants and dogs, occupy a huge mansion and enjoy themselves there.

However, let's turn around and take a look at the residents in the matchbox-like city. Five or six families have to gather in a single foreign-style house, and the middle section of the escalator is suspended in the air, commonly known by Shanghai people as the so-called "mezzanine." There, the toilet and the baggage are placed together, the parents-in-law and the sons and daughters-in-law sleep in the same room, and after the children get out of school, they have to study old books under the oil lamp, but the chirping of sparrows and the noise of scolding around will disrupt your tranquility, so every worker reduces his wages for working on the docks tomorrow due to insomnia, and every elementary school student often cannot complete their limited education due to the lack of a good environment!! There is no need to talk about the people on the roads anymore, how many laborers are sleeping on the sidewalks again! Shanghai, this Shanghai of the poor, is as dark as mud, as cold as a knife, and as foul-smelling as disinfectant!

— Zhi Qing

Learning should be like a pyramid, with common sense and all common sciences as the foundation, and specialized knowledge just like the spire.

▲ Love is a beautiful flower, blooming on cliffs, if we want to pick it, we should go through all the hardships to find it, not something that can be obtained by picking it up.

▲ Failure is a good opportunity to indicate that we should not make mistakes in the future. Honest failure is not dishonorable, but being afraid of failure is truly dishonorable.

▲ There is nothing impossible in the world, just doing it and seeing is the best move.

The Poor and the Rich

— Yan Chonglou

Now is the era of money, so it is difficult for the poor to gain a foothold in this world, while the rich have the authority to rule this world!

Some people say: "The city is heaven for the rich and hell for the poor." I say: "The city is heaven for the muddled and hell for the clear-headed."

The poor people walking hope that there are no cars on the road, and the rich people sitting in cars hope that there are no pedestrians on the road, because the poor want to walk slowly on the road, and the rich want to drive fast on the road.

Those with money rely on money and can do anything, so I say "The rich are a kind of machine." Those without money have nothing and cannot do anything, so I say "The poor are a walking corpse."

The poor become rich through diligence and frugality, and the rich become poor through extravagance and laziness. The poor become rich, and the rich become poor. This is a cycle of wealth and poverty.

Girlfriend is a Lover

Novel

Scarlet

— Shou Juan

At this time, the sun had reached its rest time, half of its body had hidden behind the horizon, leaving only a little bit of the tip of its tongue slightly exposed outside its lips. Flocks of crows in the sky were chattering one after another, as if proudly telling humans, "We are about to return to our happy and comfortable homes." Ouyang Sheng sent off these black dots of activity, and could not help but sigh softly, and so his thoughts progressed in an orderly manner.

The beginning of the second act: He barely broke through the harsh cold of the day, crossed a wilderness that seemed more vast than the Pacific Ocean, staggering and stumbling all the way, risking his life forward. He doubted several times whether there was a destination in this world that he needed at this moment. Every pore on his body was tense. Under these circumstances, he finally arrived at his destination - the home of his good friend Dongfang Sheng - but, alas, his situation at the time was actually more trembling and disheveled than a soldier who had fought hard for ten days and nights in a hail of bullets and a bloody mist. The ferocity of the wind was greater than artillery; the cruelty of the snow was greater than a quick gun; probably after a few more moments of cold and terror, he might only be able to shake hands with death, and not be able to reach the door of his beloved friend.

It was near midnight, and only wind and snow held all the authority. He crouched with his corpse-like cold body in front of Dongfang Sheng's steps, his whole body covered with snow, from a distance looking almost like a great white heron with its neck retracted and asleep. The joints of his entire body trembled in bursts, like a worn-out car racing madly, with no possibility of trembling any longer. His upper and lower teeth also started a fierce struggle, continuously doing that self-mutilating work. But he still stretched his neck and, in the northwest wind, desperately uttered a hoarse appeal. He thought that his cry was as loud as it could be, but the hateful northwest wind was even louder than his cry. And every time he opened his mouth, a large gust of wind, carrying several snowflakes, hit the side of his mouth. After some more time, heaven took pity, and when the merciful wind subsided slightly, he actually sent that pitiful sound inside. He actually summoned the souls of Dongfang Sheng and his wife from their sweet dreams. When he heard the voices of people inside the door, it was like receiving the gospel bestowed by God himself. As soon as the door opened, where could he wait to lift his foot and cross the threshold, his upper body plunged forward and fell straight into the door. (3)

Local Chronicle

Ancient City Fragments

— Peng Ruogu

Washington Irving once referred to the town of TarryTown with the name Creensburgh during his stay. I say Suzhou is a perfect fit for that description.

Geographically, there are three water towns: Venice in Italy, Bangkok, and our Suzhou. However, they can't match our Suzhou, which boasts the magnificent Tai Lake with 36,000 hectares and 72 peaks! The rest are hardly worth mentioning.

As the saying goes, "Above there is heaven, below there are Suzhou and Hangzhou." Consider that even the alluring West Lake, famous for its beauty, is inferior to Suzhou. Isn't that proof of Suzhou's fame? Westlake said, "The Qiantang River in the evening is the most delightful time to experience the beauty of the Venice of the East." I say it's not as good as the area around Seven Mile Shantang.

Ever since the poet Zhang Ji's "Night Mooring" poem was introduced to Japan, Japanese scholars, merchants, and military experts have flocked to Suzhou in batches to sightsee, paint scenery, view the maple leaves at Tianping Mountain, and visit Hanshan Temple. Riding on donkeys, they secretly planned their secret work. From the perspective of our research into the arts, the poet Zhang Ji cannot escape a huge responsibility, just as we blame Marco Polo, the author of "The Travels of Marco Polo," for the current imperialist aggression.

The bell from "Midnight Bell Rings at the Passenger Ship" can never be heard again! It was long ago stolen by those heartless Ezo people. Kang Youwei has the lines "The bell sound has crossed the sea eastwards, chilling the maple leaves of Hanshan Ancient Temple" inscribed at Maple Bridge. Ah! Listen, listen! Isn't it wailing mournfully now on the distant three islands? It's the call of the spirits of our ancient Suzhou martyrs!

The modern playwright Tian Han, in his play "Suzhou Nights," sings:

Go, go!

Go to the streets at night!

Go to Suzhou at night!

How interesting the nights of Suzhou are!

You can see the moon on the Roman-like city walls,

You can see the water in the Venetian-like streets,

You can see gondola-like boats,

You can see Gypsy-like girls on the boats,

This is a eulogy exposing the beauty of the ancient city.

During the late Ming Dynasty, Mao Yilu, a henchman of the eunuch Wei Zhongxian, came to Suzhou to serve as an official. The people rose up to drive him out. Later, Wei Zhongxian wanted to kill all the people of Suzhou. The righteous men Yan Peiwei and four others boldly took responsibility for that uprising. In the end, they were killed! Such a great tragedy, in the Suzhou city with its weak popular sentiment, can be said to be the only one. But now the graves of the five righteous men have become so dilapidated that they are unrecognizable! I hope the local gentry and members of the Antiquities Preservation Association will be responsible for renovating them.

The modern playwright Tian Han has a play called "Blood and Snow."

It depicts the story of the five Suzhou martyrs who died in the late Ming Dynasty. Its value is comparable to "One Heart."

Women are also one of Suzhou's specialties. But in the end, they are evil! Thousands of years ago, our Suzhou was destroyed by Xi Shi. Now the Qin Terrace, Echo Corridor, and Xi Shi Cave on Lingyan Mountain are all vestiges of her sins!

As far as I know, Suzhou has two tomb inscriptions that are worthy of appreciation by those who love literature and art. One is at the foot of Lingyan Mountain, belonging to the poet Zhang Yongfu, with the words "Tomb of the One Who Returns." The other is the living tomb that the monk Da Xiu prepared for himself during his lifetime on Little Huang Mountain (?). The inscription on the stele reads "Da Xiu's Resting Place." Suzhou is known as a residential area, but the most regrettable shortcoming is the lack of tap water. Every household still drinks well water and river water. The well water always has a salty taste, and dead dogs and cats often fall into the river water, plus daily excrement. Drinking it is really unhygienic. This is something that the people of Suzhou must find a way to improve.

Free Talk

The Funeral of the Humorist Chekhov

— Shi Jingxie

Everyone knows that Chekhov was a relatively short-lived writer. On July 2, 1904, he fell ill from tuberculosis and passed away in Germany. His remains were immediately transported from Germany to Moscow. On the day the remains arrived in Moscow, the Moscow station was almost completely occupied by people welcoming the spirit. Soon, the train arrived, and a coffin was carried down from a green freight car. A troop of soldiers saluted the coffin with great respect. Although the people welcoming Chekhov's coffin felt very strange, they had no choice but to follow behind the coffin. Later, they found out they were wrong. That was the remains of General Kairell, who died in Manchuria in the Russo-Japanese War, while the coffin of the humorist Chekhov was carried down from another freight car. The body of that freight car clearly read: "Carriage for Transporting Pigs"! Isn't this deliberately joking with Chekhov?

Regarding the funeral that day, Gorky wrote in his diary:

"At most, no more than a hundred people followed Chekhov's coffin to the funeral, certainly not more. At that time, the two lawyers among the mourners made me think the most. Both of them were wearing new shoes and knotted ties, obviously both 'engaged.' I followed behind these two mourners, listening to the one called Mark Kontarkov discussing the cleverness and stupidity of dogs: the other, whom I didn't know, was boasting about how comfortable his country villa was and how beautiful the surrounding scenery was. There was also a woman wearing a wisteria-colored dress and holding a parasol decorated with green lace, chattering to an old gentleman wearing large glasses about the virtues of the deceased Chekhov: 'Do you know, he was a very charming person, and not a single word he said wasn't humorous and funny!' The old man seemed to disagree, only coughing softly. That day, the weather was very hot, and dust was flying. At the front of the funeral, a burly patrolman rode a fat white horse, leading the way triumphantly."

Finally, Gorky ended his recollections of the great writer's funeral with a kind of intense mockery:

"Everything, everything, was too extraordinarily ordinary and vulgar, which is really too much for the memory of such a great and skillful writer!"

This is the funeral of the humorist Chekhov. If Chekhov had a spirit, I wonder what kind of humorous and stern tone he would use in his coffin to respond to this social teasing!

The Generals' Sufferings

— Fan Zhongyun

Following the news of the fall of Yuguan, we saw many impassioned telegrams and speeches in the newspapers. Zhang Xueliang's speech was: He would "defend justice with blood and flesh, return our territory, everything is possible." Zhang Xueliang, who advocated non-resistance, is now determined to resist. Generals such as Yan Xishan, Han Fuju, Song Zheyuan, Xu Yuanquan, He Chengjun, and Cai Tingkai all volunteered one after another, willing to be the vanguard in resisting Japan. Even Liu Xiang, who was busy with internal warfare, telegraphed a statement "ending military affairs, ready to fight."

From the occurrence of the September 18th Incident until today, the situation of "friendship" and "peace" maintained in the face of enemy artillery fire and slaughter is bound to be broken. The battle of Shanhaiguan has ultimately become the fuse for the Sino-Japanese War, I think. However, more than a week has passed since the fall of Yuguan, and the front line at Shihe is calm. The newspapers are always spreading news of mediation, but things don't seem to be about to explode into war. Our policy toward Japan still seems to be calm, forbearance, and non-resistance.

General He Zhuguo said: "No war, no peace, no defense, no retreat, later generations will know the hardships." But in addition to General He's hardships, I know that the other generals also have their own hardships. Because "war is fierce and dangerous," especially resisting the powerful Japan is not a child's play after all. It must be fought with one's own life and territory. Look: Ma Zhanshan resisted in Longjiang, and failed. Cai Tingkai resisted in Shanghai, and withdrew his troops. Su Bingwen resisted in Manzhouli, and retreated into Russia. This time, He Zhuguo in Shanhaiguan, the result of a fierce battle, was that the magnificent pass and natural barrier turned to ashes, and he retreated to Shihe. What benefits are there to resistance? On the contrary, after the "Shanghai Truce Agreement," Shanghai still did not lose its status as a "entertainment saves the country" Shanghai. Why bother to resist?

Therefore, what unfolds with the Shanhaiguan Incident is definitely not a hot war of blood and fire. Please rest assured, people of the ancient country who "love peace"! Moreover, the Shanhaiguan resistance may be the last resistance. Soon, after the Shanhaiguan truce is "arranged" and "agreed," the foundation of "East Asian peace" will still be as stable as Mount Tai.

Red Bean

— Cao Juren

The modern poet Liu Dabai has a connection with red beans.

These small, crimson, and slightly purple beans symbolize the flames burning in his heart.

On New Year's Day in 1924, he received a pair of red beans from Zhou Gangzhi in Jiangyin and wrote three poems for them:

"At the beginning of the year," a letter, carefully sealed with two pearls, affectionately called red beans. The tree is all withered, but resurrected, fearing there are no seeds of longing, heaven leaves half a stock.

Looking south of the river, the tree is withered, don't look at it as an ordinary old tree, longing is conveyed by this. The body is slightly round, the color is slightly red, the starlight and rosy clouds shine in the sky, the scattered red is pitiful.

A pair of beans, a pair of people, red beans stored in a brocade bag, an old friend in a distant land. Like the heart, in the heart, tightly hidden in the heart, let not separation grow long.

He loved this charming object with deep sentimental charm, keeping it in his sleeve and playing with it endlessly. Last spring, Mr. Liu Dabai passed away, and the pair of red beans, I don't know where they have fallen. On the third day after his death, a girl in red came to touch the coffin and cry, and everyone did not know her. Asking her the reason, she revealed herself to be Mr. Liu Dabai's "sweetheart," saying that they had loved each other deeply; later, she took out the red beans as proof. This pair of red beans has finally found a home.

Mr. Dabai asked Zhou Gangzhi to help him find anecdotes about red beans in the Jiangyin County Records, but Zhou Gangzhi was soon executed in Jiangyin on suspicion of being a reactionary, and there was no further news. Mr. Dabai himself found the poems and lyrics of Wan Hongyou and Wang Biguo, Qu Dajun's "Wooden Language," Niu Xiu's "Yue Gu," Zhou Liangong's "Book Shadow," and other anecdotes. As far as I know, the "Sou Shen Ji" has a record:

"The wife of the official Han Ping was beautiful, and King Kang of Song seized her. Ping committed suicide, and his wife threw herself off the tower and died. The king was angry and ordered them to be buried so that they could not see each other. Overnight, a catalpa tree grew from both ends of the two graves, its roots intertwined below and its branches intertwined above. King Song mourned them and named the tree the 'Thinking of Each Other Tree.'"

This story is as sad and beautiful as the story recorded in Niu Xiu's "Yue Gu."

Among the poems about red beans, Wang Wei's "Red beans grow in the south, how many branches sprout in spring: I wish you would pick more, this thing is the most for longing" is the most famous. Wen Tingyun's poem, "Exquisite dice inlaid with red beans, does anyone know the bone-deep longing," is also widely circulated.

New Sextant

— Xia Qiu

A sextant is an instrument commonly used in navigation or surveying. By measuring the angle of the sun with it, the direction of the ship's course can be determined. Sextants used in the past required sunlight to measure their angles, and once fog or clouds covered the sun, the sextant basically lost its effectiveness. The new sextant is different. Even in heavy fog, it can still measure the height of the sun. Its principle is as follows: We know that the sun has infrared rays (infrared Rayss). These rays can pass through any kind of cloud or fog, but they cannot be seen by the naked eye. Only a photoelectric cell (Photo-Eltclric Cell) can collect them and make them appear on the lens. The new sextant is equipped with a specially made photoelectric tube. The infrared rays from the sun can directly shine on its telescope, so it can be used whether the sun is hidden or visible.

Strange Japanese Marriage Customs

— Chen Shi

The term "marriage" (結婚) in ancient Japan, called Mitonomakhay, or Kunag, or Yoby (transliteration), simply referred to sexual intercourse between men and women, or a man going to a woman's house for a secret rendezvous. This usage has a long history in Japanese customs, and many strange marriage customs can be inferred from these words. Now, there are not many remnants of such strange customs in Japan, so the general usage that is popular today will gradually become incomprehensible and become mysterious and archaic. This is probably due to the prohibition by the Japanese authorities or natural abolition! But it is not entirely true to say that their traditions have all disappeared. Here, let's talk about those traditions!

In a certain village on Awaji Island, on the eve of the wedding, the groom's most trusted friend first sleeps with the bride. This is probably a tradition of the so-called "avoidance of virginity" or "right of the first night." It has the same origin as the story of the village chief of Yomyo Village, Hetsuku County, in the northern part of Bungo Province, exercising his "right of the first night" over all the young women in the village on the night of August 16th. A similar custom is also prevalent in northeastern Hokkaido.

In the Ishigaki Island area of ​​the Great Ryukyu, there is also a custom of using a handkerchief stained with menstrual blood as an engagement gift. I remember Dr. Ernst Vatter's "Ritural and Peliein Morocco. Voli." also described a strange custom of Moroccan men and women getting engaged, which coincides with the Japanese custom of menstrual blood handkerchiefs. He said that Moroccan women, when they reach the age of love, firmly believe in this superstition. They believe that when they miss their lover, they only need to cut off a little of their pubic hair and armpit hair, burn it, or burn a handkerchief stained with menstrual blood, and recite a specific incantation, and it will immediately take effect, and the lover will definitely come to meet her secretly. This point can prove that there are many places in the customs of the East and the West that can be connected. The girls of Ishigaki Island in Ryukyu give their boyfriends a handkerchief stained with their own menstrual blood as a token of engagement.

There is also the marriage custom of Izu Oshima in Japan. When the bride is in the midst of the most lively wedding ceremony, she must sneak back to her mother's house, and she must not be known by the guests or all the people of the husband's family. If the bride cannot sneak away during the most lively wedding ceremony, she will be laughed at or scorned by the entire village. This custom of the bride sneaking away can very well prove that it is a residual concept of women who were robbed during the era of marriage by capture and still wanted to escape back.

There is also the marriage custom of Amami Oshima, where the groom's family first sends a messenger to the bride's house to welcome the bride. All the tricks are strung together by this messenger. He drinks heavily and sings loudly in the bride's house, and the songs are mostly teasing words. After a night of noise, the bride is welcomed back together to hold the wedding the next day.

A Certain Person's Sorrow

— Yang Xingzhi

This world is like being pushed into a pitch-black abyss. The sun has no light and no heat since that year. The sea is howling, the wind is wailing, the world is trembling in the darkness, and everywhere you look there is gunpowder, everywhere there are living landmines.

××××

Raising the whip, the world no longer obeys my command. Looking at the piles of goods, I can only sigh. Damn it! That group of people who can't starve to death or freeze to death still desperately make trouble: they want work, they want food.

××××

I heard that a group of people who can't starve to death once demonstrated in front of the solemn White House. I heard that the magnificent London was also surrounded by a group of people who can't freeze to death.

Our knives, guns, sticks, and gas bombs no longer have any power now.

Riots, uprisings, and annoying shouts have actually run into "our society"!

××××

I look up to the sky and ask: What is your intention?

Stretching out my hand, the glory of the past cannot be recalled.

Everything has changed, everything has changed since that year.

Heaven, I can only tremble at your feet!

Long Novel

The Crossroads of Era and Love (Continued)

— Zhang Ziping

Madam Hezi did not recognize Haiquan as a remarkable handsome man either. However, she was interested in his strong masculinity and not entirely uninhibited attitude.

She lightened her footsteps and walked to his bedside.

"Mr. Lin;"

She called out softly with a smile. Of course, there was no response. She really wanted to wake him up and have a long chat with her, because she hadn't seen him for several days, and she felt a little attached to him. But just for a moment, after thinking about it, she didn't have the courage. She just stood by his bed and daydreamed, and suddenly smelled a burst of alcohol. She saw Haiquan yawn in the quilt, turned over, and his face was facing outward. She thought he was awake, and her heart jumped. But Haiquan still didn't know that there was an intruder standing by his bed, and fell asleep again.

"That's right. He went to Ren's house to drink tonight and came back."

So she lightened her footsteps and walked to the table again. Shen Bao Local Supplement

Remarks

Anecdotes in the Japanese Education Circle

— Bai Tao

Discipline Director Works as a Prostitute

Professor's Wife Drives a Taxi to Pick Up Passengers

A few months ago, we saw in the newspapers that a female teacher in Dongying Island was working as a prostitute. Recently, the wife of a Kyoto Imperial University professor can even drive a taxi to pick up passengers. These are all anecdotes in the Japanese education circle. The reporter is not very clear about the female teacher working as a prostitute, but probably that female teacher was working as a discipline director in a certain ordinary elementary school. Because the education industry is poor and the salary she received was not enough for her to spend, the smart female teacher came up with a special way to make money: she behaved properly and went to school to work as a discipline director during the day, and at night she put on makeup and went to a coffee shop to pick up customers. Moreover, she was actually able to have a bustling business and triple her profits, and she became generous. Later, this unfortunate female teacher was arrested by the military police and fired by the school authorities. According to the Japanese themselves, it was because she committed a great crime of desecrating the sacred education industry.

Regarding the professor's wife who recently drove a taxi to pick up passengers, the Kyoto telegraph in Japan said this: In the Gion Kujo area of ​​Kyoto, there are noble women driving jeep taxis and frequently calling for passengers, which is quite eye-catching. After investigation, it was learned that the lady was Ritsuko, 32 years old, the wife of Kizo Ubukawa, an assistant professor in the Department of Economics at Kyoto Imperial University. Mrs. Ritsuko secretly practiced and obtained a driver's license because her husband was devoted to research and did not produce anything. She worked as a driver during the day to make a profit and as a housewife at night to manage the household, hoping to help her husband complete his studies. This Mrs. Ritsuko is really rare, rare! Professor Kizo Ubukawa can get a virtuous assistant!

I think Mrs. Ritsuko is very likely to have committed the crime of "hindering public morals," but perhaps the Japanese military police will forgive her because of her commendable ambition!

Our Chinese student circles have also had similar things happen. For example, students in a certain school in Suzhou used to pull rickshaws. Recently, Ms. Wang Yurong, a female student at Jinghua Middle School in Nanjing, worked as a singer in Confucius Temple, and unfortunately, Ms. Wang was fired by the principal for working as a singer. This can also be considered an anecdote in the education circle.

Science

Artificial Ivory

— Luxhuang

Artificial ivory has many uses, and because it is cheap and beautiful, its sales have exceeded those of real ivory several times.

There are many methods for making artificial ivory, and the products are different. The most common one is made from formaldehyde and carbolic acid, named bakelite. The artificial ivory described in this article is made from a waste product, and its value is cheaper than bakelite. The manufacturing method of carbolic acid ivory will be described later.

After milk has been stored for a long time, there is a substance floating on the surface, like scale, which is called cheese. Ordinary people only regard it as waste from milk, but they do not know that artificial ivory, which has a wide range of applications, is made from this as raw material.

The industry of using cheese to make ivory was invented in 1897 and has been improved many times. Products were first launched on the market in 1900. Its products can replace products made of horns, hawksbill turtle shells, etc. When used as a substitute for celluloid, although its elasticity is not as strong as the latter, it is non-combustible and can also be used as a raw material for making children's toys. It can also insulate electricity and is often used in electrical materials. Other products include umbrella handles, fountain pen barrels, brush boards, combs, mirror frames, and many other varieties. The manufacturing method is introduced below.

First, use acids (such as acetic acid) to precipitate the cheese in the milk to remove other ingredients from the milk. Then add water and alkalis to the cheese and heat it to 100 degrees Celsius, stirring it while heating it until it becomes a thick colloidal liquid. At this time, the desired color can be added. Afterwards, add extremely dilute hydrochloric acid. After adding it, stir it for a long time, and then put it into various molds to press it into the shape of an object. However, this kind of product shows cracks when it dries, so after twelve hours, put the above-mentioned product into formaldehyde and take it out after a while. Not only does the nature of the finished product become hard, but also there are no cracks when it dries. It does not absorb water when immersed in water, and is much more exquisite than crude products.

Literature and Art

Returning Home to Show My Wife

— Wu Tiansheng

A dream of boats and carts has sent off autumn. True laughter at chasing fame and fortune with a whip. I pity you for saving the family and measuring rice. The broken stove labors with firewood, cooking sorrow together. Also teach the children to rely on spinning and weaving. Again, I am shocked by the war, fleeing many times. Returning, ten thousand calamities disperse like clouds. Carrying and watching the reunion, the moon is full on the building.

Frost Goose

Breaking through sorrow, flying ten thousand miles in the darkness. The reflection shines on the passes and rivers, solemn all around. The spirits of those who appealed can be connected remotely. What is the point of leaving mud and melon behind? Crossing the sky, carrying a stern spirit. Arrayed, there is still a stern power. From beyond the border, a cold wind signal is tight. Ashamed in the cold, the rice and millet are abundant.

The Family of a "Bumi" (Local Chinese) Mistress

— Yi Lie

Our second landlord can be described as someone who appears in shadow plays. She is a chubby woman in her thirties. Her attitude towards tenants is also like a performance in a shadow play. She has a kind face for wealthy tenants and a ferocious face for those without money.

Although past her prime, she still possesses some charm. When she puts on makeup, she looks exactly like a modern young woman. Their family structure is generally like this: there is a seventy-year-old grandmother, a five or six-year-old son, a twelve or thirteen-year-old maid, and an old nanny.

I really can't determine who the male head of their family is. From what I know, there is a man around fifty years old and a man around thirty years old wearing a smart Western suit, who often come. And they often spend the night at the second landlord's place. But I never see the old and young ones coming at the same time, so I was obviously wrong to guess they were father and son.

According to the maid's address, she calls the older one "Big Master" and the younger one "Master." Of course, this cannot be taken as evidence to say that these are the second landlord's husband and young lover. I have tried all sorts of methods to find out the truth about the second landlord's family structure, but after spending a long time, I got no results at all.

One afternoon at two o'clock, the man in the smart Western suit came. The second landlord said:

"Why are you here today?"

"Okay, don't be so anxious."

Then she made a phone call. The call went through:

"Hello! Where is this?"

"Is this ×× Jewelry Shop? Ask Boss Wang to answer the phone."

"Is this Wang ××?"

"Don't come today, I have something to do and won't be back until twelve o'clock at night."

She hung up the receiver, returned to the room, closed the door, and I don't know what she was doing.

Things in the world are so coincidental.

One afternoon at five o'clock, the man in the smart Western suit came again, but our second landlord had already gone out.

About twenty minutes later, the second landlord returned in a car with a man in his fifties, bringing many things out of the car.

Nothing could make her more hesitant and uneasy than now. I really can't describe it. However, our second landlord is always a clever woman. She immediately turned her hesitation and uneasiness into an attitude of surprise and called out:

Page 18

"Cousin, when did you come?"

"This is my cousin," then turning her head she said, "This is your cousin-in-law."

Driven by curiosity, I spent all my energy and finally got a little bit of a clue.

The Authoritative Child

— Mi Lu

He's probably fourteen or fifteen years old. The child at the delivery desk of the ×× Studio speaks a Sichuan accent that's neither here nor there, and sometimes he even speaks Shanghai dialect. Although he's not very educated, he knows the first names of the girls and jumps around very actively. If there's anything to be done, he does it for people very quickly. In everyone's eyes, he's indeed a well-behaved child.

The waiting room is almost full of guests every day. Those who arrive later have to wait anxiously outside, hoping for a vacant seat. Especially on Saturday afternoons, the sound of laughter is no different from a teahouse. The only difference is that people are sitting around, and there are candies and melon seeds on the table, but no teapots or teacups.

According to the rules of the waiting room, it's open until 7 PM every night except Saturdays. Saturdays are specially extended to 9 PM. Although it's extended by two hours, the male students seem reluctant to leave, sitting there as if the rules hanging on the wall are just empty words to them.

The well-behaved child comes running, touching the light switch, as if he can't bear to separate him and her. But the time is up, otherwise, it seems like he's not doing his job. Finally, with a "click," he says, "Lights out!"

Everyone's conversation suddenly stops, and they disperse without any doubt.

The well-behaved child actually wields such great authority!

He is truly an "authoritative child."

(7) Today's universities don't seem like gardens for "seeking knowledge," but rather places for "seeking mates."

(8) Embedding a few unnecessary English words in works or conversations is considered the most beautiful thing by modern people.

Gone Mad?

— Chen Zhou

The clock struck four times, and Mother Wang knew it was time for school to end. She hurriedly put down the needlework in her hand, ran to the stove, told Ah Jin to light the coal stove, rolled up her sleeves, washed vegetables, and cut glutinous rice cakes, preparing refreshments, waiting for her sixteen-year-old son Lang to come home to eat.

"Mom," sure enough, her son Lang came home! But the voice of calling Mom didn't seem as cheerful and clear as it used to be, just heavy and sluggish. Lang put down his schoolbag, sat on the chair next to the table, his face like an iron plate, without saying a word.

"Lang! Are you hungry?" Mom asked.

".................................."

"Why don't you say anything? Are you hungry?... You..."

"Did you quarrel with a classmate?" Mom guessed.

"No, Mom."

"Then why aren't you happy? Are you feeling unwell?"

"No, Mom! I want to join the army!"

"What?"

"I want to join the army! The Japanese are too hateful! They've occupied our Shanhaiguan! And killed countless of our loyal and brave volunteers and innocent compatriots!

It's hateful that those heartless compatriots of ours are actually buying Japanese goods in large quantities, otherwise how could the import of Japanese goods continue to increase sharply? Alas! The Changsha June 1st Massacre, the May 30th Incident, Jinan, ... ... ... the September 18th Incident, ... ... ... the January 28th Incident, there are too many massacres! They were born and live under the massacres! They are used to it, yes, we can't blame them! But whose fault is this? Mom! I can't be as numb as they are, at least I want to show that I am a member of the Republic of China, join the army! Fight! Drive out the Japanese dwarfs!" Lang said loudly and passionately.

"Be quiet! Lang, I don't know what your teacher said to you today, making you go crazy!" Mom complained about the teacher.

"No, I'm not crazy! I want to join the army! The teacher's words are not wrong at all! Mom, look! In the world, except for China, which country is not making progress: Turkey after the European War! India, forgetting its country! And all the small countries challenging the imperialists! The dignified Republic of China, at this critical moment of survival, doesn't save itself, resist! If you say: this is learning from India, then why isn't Japan afraid of you? Moreover, open your eyes and see, has China already forgotten its country, you need to calm down, wait until after forgetting your country before you calm down, it won't be too late! At that time, if you don't calm down, your master will tell you to calm down! But, now the country hasn't been forgotten yet! Mom, I don't want to be complacent, I... ... I want to join the army!" Lang rushed downstairs like a madman.

"Ah Jin! Quickly stop the young master! Don't let him run away!" Mother Wang shouted while running downstairs. "I want to join the army!" Lang cried, and Mother Wang and Ah Jin carried him to Mother Wang's bedroom.

The Argument in the Self-Study Room

— Wu Wei

This was the first day after the New Year holiday. The class bell hadn't rung yet, and there were only me and SL in the self-study room, so the air was very quiet. Ten minutes later, M came in, just stepping through the door; his mouth was already shouting, "What books are you reading! It's almost the anniversary"!

"What's called the anniversary?" L was the first to look up and say.

"Yuguan fell!... Look, Shanghai is also almost having an anniversary," M said enthusiastically. At the same time, as if to confirm this, he said: "Isn't someone moving in Zhabei again?"

"Okay, don't anniversary or not anniversary, I know what you mean: you think you have money, and in case something happens, you can run to the concession: live your dance hall life, right?" Our patriotic youth S said.

"Of course!" M said, making a face. But, then he continued, "If you don't enjoy yourself in time, do you have to wait until the country is destroyed to enjoy yourself?"

"You cold-blooded ××!" S said angrily.

"Don't say it! Looking at the current situation, if I didn't have two nostrils, I would have died of anger! At first, when the thieves came, they didn't resist, but when they had already entered the door and wanted to come to the living room, then there was so-called resistance. But, the difference in weapons is pitiful, and Yuguan finally fell. Even more ridiculous, the people behind the living room are still killing each other! The League of Nations' help to us is already very clear, but there are still people who believe in it. If this goes on, wouldn't it be better to simply destroy the country?"

M said a lot of nonsense.

"I see you talking about the destruction of the country all the time. When the country is really destroyed, will you still have such happiness and freedom as you have now?... The Northeast Volunteer Army is resisting because they don't want to be slaves to a destroyed country, and also because they can't stand the tragic sight of a destroyed country. According to your way of spending money, although I don't want you to destroy your family to help the country, you should donate a little more money to the Volunteer Army. Last time when you donated to the Volunteer Army, it was painful to see you take out four dimes?... "S thought of M's stingy appearance when donating money last time and became more and more angry.

"Then since you are so patriotic, why don't you go to the Northeast to fight?" S said.

"Although I don't go to the Northeast, I won't go to the dance hall during the national crisis," M said, at the same time, he shielded M with his hand, which was obviously a sign of challenge.

"A poor ghost like you isn't qualified to enter a dance hall!" M said, twisting his mouth.

S was extremely angry at this time and was ready to act freely, M was also clenching his fists ready to resist! At this time, L, who was sitting next to him, quickly dragged S away: saying that if you want to fight, go fight the dwarfs! Don't also play the game of fighting among ourselves, coincidentally the bell rang, so they each took their books to take the big exam, I followed behind them, walking and thinking, it was really funny and infuriating, I didn't expect people who received university education to say such nonsense, and the so-called patriots would also do this trick of fighting among themselves, and fighting their own people, alas! Patriotic youths, Chinese students.

Correspondence from Store Employees

The Method of "Looking for a Horse While Riding One"

Mr. Editor:

After reading Mr. Wu's letter "Recognizing a Thief as a Father and Being in a Dilemma" on January 8th, I deeply sympathize with him. However, I don't think your answer is very satisfactory. Because your answer is "Resignation is the right thing to do, and as for the future problems, as long as you are willing to endure hardship, it is not difficult to solve your personal life." But Mr. Wu's letter has already mentioned "There are no relatives or friends in Shanghai." If he resigns, he will have no relatives or friends to turn to, and his finances will inevitably be difficult! Food and lodging will become a problem. Even if he lives in a small inn and eats pancakes and fried dough sticks, it will cost at least forty cents a day. If he finds a job within one or two days, that's fine, but if he can't find one, how will he support himself after a long time?

So my humble opinion is: while you haven't resigned yet, it's better to temporarily endure the humiliation in order to wait for a good opportunity to come. On the one hand, encourage yourself in the store, and on the other hand, pay attention to advertisements in the newspaper for trainee positions, etc., and work hard to take the exam. After passing the exam, then resign from your original position. This is the so-called "looking for a horse while riding one" method, so that you don't fall into extreme difficulty. What do you gentlemen think?

Respectfully, Wu Dingxin, January 9th

Editor's Note: After reading the above letter, we are very impressed with Mr. Wu's deep thinking and careful planning. We also welcome his suggestion of different opinions and further planning of practical methods.

However, we believe that this "looking for a horse while riding one" method is good, of course! But from the standpoint of the nation, it can be used to find a way out because you are dissatisfied with the bad environment in the stubborn store, but it cannot be used in Japanese stores, which have always been regarded as enemies.

We still remember: during the fierce "January 28th" Songhu bloody battle last year, a driver named Hu Amao drove a car full of enemy military supplies and with four enemy soldiers escorting the car into the Huangpu River! He exchanged the lives of four enemies for the life of one person, and added tens of thousands of dollars worth of military supplies. This spirit of sacrificing oneself is a true manifestation of the Chinese national character! This spirit! It has won unanimous praise from the whole country and even the world! After a year, our impression is still very deep.

Now, the Volunteer Army outside the Pass is fighting bloody battles with the enemy in the snowy and icy land. Although they have difficulty with supplies and lack clothing and food, they are not tempted by the enemy's huge amount of money: although they lack follow-up support and have weak troops, they are not threatened by the enemy's heavy artillery fire: their perseverance and unyielding behavior, and their commendable actions, the manifestation of national character, and the spirit of fearless sacrifice; have also won the sympathy of the people of the whole country and the praise of people all over the world!

In this way, what does personal sacrifice count for? We must stand on our position, carry forward our inherent national character, and absolutely not cooperate with our enemies: this is our humble intention in answering Mr. Wu.

Based on the above point of view, we also feel that although Mr. Wu has temporarily gained material comfort in the enemy's store, he is suffering tremendously in spirit. (See Mr. Wu's own statement) So we resolutely told him "Resignation is the right thing to do"; as for Mr. Wu after resignation, then we should find another way, we would rather starve to death, and never should we serve the enemy. We have no power to help solve the problem of food and lodging, but we believe that if Mr. Wu has the determination to "rather starve to death than live in dishonor," he will definitely get help from the society. If society cannot help, it is the people of the country who have failed Mr. Wu, and Mr. Wu has not failed the nation! If Mr. Wu does not have this determination, we dare not advise him to resign.

Novel

Sympathizers, Continued XV

— Zhang Henshui

This landlord was originally a gentleman, but because the power of the township autonomous region has been transferred to the new-school young gentry, he has no connection at all. Because of a small matter, he was caught by the district and severely fined. Moreover, he also sent a heavy gift to the gentlemen in the district. Only then did he realize that the new school people were more powerful in raising money than the old school people, and he simply didn't dare to provoke the people in the autonomous region. Now that Meng Guobao mentioned the district again, he was a little scared, so he didn't dare to say strong words anymore. He pulled one of the people who ate with him over and asked him to intercede, saying good things and bad things, and stipulating that Wang Laoer would pay two more dan of rice. If there was no rice, he would pay ten yuan. This was a happy surprise for Wang Laoer, and he agreed to everything, because he expected to pay at least twenty yuan. After this negotiation was over, everyone dispersed, and Meng Guobao also bid farewell. Wang Laoer helped the second sister-in-law wash the bowls and pots in the kitchen. Seeing that there were still a dozen or twenty melon seeds on the windowsill, he asked: Who left these melon seeds? Laoer said it unintentionally, but the second sister-in-law's face turned red. She said: Who do you think left them? There won't be a second person in the kitchen. You really don't know how to talk. Wang Laoer laughed: It's not worth getting angry over this, right? He said, accompanying her to wash the dishes and clean the floor. But he thought that he had offended the cook with just a word, and if he ignored her, she would get angry again, so he found something to say and said to the second sister-in-law: Hey! Do you think Mr. Meng San is good? He just said this casually, but when the second sister-in-law Wang heard it, her heart skipped a beat, her face turned red, but she couldn't work. Wang Laoer didn't know that there was another reason for this, and still looked down and said: Mr. Meng San is really good. In previous years, when the landlord came to settle accounts, many middlemen would talk at once, and they could never say anything. This year, Mr. Meng San touched his face, and in a few words, he talked away most of the rent rice. He said that he sympathized with people like us who grow fields, and I didn't believe it before, but now it seems that people are telling the truth. After he explained it again, the second sister-in-law Wang understood what he meant and said very casually; He was just happy for a while. Wang Laoer said: Don't talk nonsense, he really has a good heart and wants to be friends with me. Haven't you seen that he always talks with me until midnight these past two nights? But the second sister-in-law Wang didn't answer.

Republic of China Year 22, January 12th, Thursday, No Extra Charge

Overseas News

Consumer Cooperative in Hollywood

— Mei Cun

American capitalism is developed and the economy is affluent, but looking back at society, the unemployed are still calling for relief in groups. The number of people is not uncommon compared to other countries. In Hollywood's film industry, this recession is inevitable. Therefore, many stars initiated, based on the spirit of cooperation, and raised funds to establish a consumer cooperative and open stores to benefit their peers in purchasing.

Most of the various things sold in the store are made by out-of-school girls from poor families. Other things like furniture, antiques, and evening dresses and shoes and socks owned by stars are donated voluntarily. Small actors and others who do odd jobs have very difficult lives. Buying things in this store is very cheap, which can reduce a little burden economically.

The staff in the store are all filled by the wives or daughters of the stars. Their background, of course, is not for the sake of the bread problem. They are completely fulfilling their obligations to society, so that the poor can get universal grace. The stars themselves, standing and watching them do business, often use various games such as throwing pots in the tea room to pass the time, arousing a lot of interest from customers.

The money earned by the cooperative is entirely used for charity. There are many actresses who have children at home but cannot afford to hire maids. When she is filming, she cannot take care of her children at the same time, which is quite difficult. Therefore, the cooperative has specially hired many female nurses to take care of their children. There are many toys available here. Walt Disney even drew funny cartoons for them to play.

In addition, there are many other places where they have the opportunity to implement relief. If you open their record book, you can see a glimpse of the contents.

Film Reviews

"Remaining Life" Six Hours to Live, Screening in Nanjing

— Ming

This is an "ordinary" film that gives us a "deep impression"!

The representative of a small country argues alone with the great powers in the League of Nations in Geneva, saving his country from the brink of ruin. The hostile country wants to pass a motion when the meeting is closed. Therefore, in his residence, he is strangled with a rope. Fortunately, a great scientist has newly invented a machine that can bring the dead back to life, but the effect only lasts for six hours? This diplomat is resurrected under the authority of science. He knows the shortness of his life, and that his lover does not know this tragic change, so he decides to persuade her to love his rival. In the end, he also vetoed the League of Nations' motion. The plot, we can say that it is too distorted, but at the same time, it cannot be said that it is not full of ideals. The first third of the whole film is inevitably stagnant, but the last two-thirds are full of stimulation and vitality. Warner Baxter plays the hero of this small country representative in the remaining six hours of his life. He has a deep, calm, and determined performance. After persuading his lover in the garden to love his rival, he sadly took out the rose that she had just given him! Warner died and she still thought he would accompany him to a banquet and personally send it to the Chinese servant! And the kissing of flowers at the time of death, meeting a female thief on the road and giving her all the money, and meeting a poor young girl and asking about her dead sister, how touching it is. John Bowers, although only a few scenes, made a good contribution. The heroine is the newly discovered British girl Marlene Gordon, who also does not lose her status.

"Air Mail Bandit Blood" is produced by Universal Pictures of the United States, with air mail as the theme and the service spirit of airmen as the description of the evolution of the story, which is quite tense. It is being screened at 　　　 starting today.

Continued News on the Screening of Soviet Films in Shanghai

— Shi Yi

The famous Soviet films "Road to Life" and "Two Meetings" will soon be screened in Shanghai. This news was obtained from Mr. Sayediez, the manager of the Soviet Film Company in Shanghai. Mr. Sa has just returned to Shanghai from Nanjing. He said that the above two films have been approved by the Central Film Inspection Committee and allowed to be screened. "Two Meetings" will be screened first. The film is directed by Urinov and the subject matter and photography and sound are excellent. "Road to Life" has been screened in 27 countries and has been shown in Paris for six months. It is very popular. It was produced by the young director Nikolai Eke, describing the life of vagrants in old Russia. Both films are realistic works, based on the real life of Russia, and were praised when reviewed in Nanjing.

Legal Observations on "Conscience"

— Qi Ying

Columbia Company's productions have always been the patent of Guanglu. However, recently, its productions have also appeared in cinemas under the United Company. It is a relatively new company, so it has very special features in terms of new ideas and trends. Of course, it has no historical constraints and nothing old to guard.

The recently released "Conscience" Attorney for the Defense at the Cathay Theater, if judged from an artistic point of view, Edmund Lowe plays a retired lawyer, his eloquence and attitude are really amazing. Because of the continuity of the play's purpose, he often has places with a cold and humorous meaning. Very few supporting actors appear, so there is nothing to talk about. The merits and demerits of the director are equal and not worth praise or criticism, but I think this film is excellent, it has other outstanding strengths!

What I am talking about is the skill and purpose of this film. It can point out the importance of the position occupied by law in the mid-20th century, and attack the weaknesses of modern law. In Chinese films, law is never mentioned at all. Even in foreign films, the descriptions of law, courts, and courts are mostly based on the parties involved in the litigation as the main body, so there is bound to be some bias in observation. A film is too much of an exception. It enters the skin of the law and makes an in-depth study of the inside story, exposing the current judicial inside story of the country without adding any false colors. It clearly states that a lawyer can play with jurors and judges rely on eloquent arguments to turn the case around in their hands. The law in modern times has extreme shortcomings and can never call out injustice for the weak.

Of course, it describes the weakness of "Anglo-American law," based on precedents. But I believe that the "statutory law" adopted by China also has considerable errors. This film also proves that the perfection of the law must be sought from the lawyers themselves. If lawyers do not reform, the law will not improve.

If you like to watch legal films, then this is the only good film. However, there are too many legal professional terms and "precedents" in it, which inevitably reduces interest. But I hope that the judges, jurists, and lawyers in Shanghai, especially those who study "Anglo-American law," will go and see it, because it is a useful practical reference book.

Audience Comments: A Discussion on "The Tramp"

— Sheng Hong

Recently, amidst the warming atmosphere of the northern war clouds, the Grand Theater and the Lyceum Theatre simultaneously premiered RKO Pictures' excellent film, "The Tramp," the latest masterpiece by the comedic genius Will Rogers. The film's entire concept is novel, the leading actor's performance is humorous and satirical, and the female lead, Madge Evans, is a rising star who demonstrates significant progress in her acting. Her exquisite and lively demeanor greatly contributes to the development of the plot. Will Rogers plays the role of a tramp in this film, a wanderer returning from the battlefield, "boundless as the vast, sandy plain..."

The general plot describes a young man who leaves his wife to join the army. His delicate wife, unaccustomed to cold nights, ventures out to seek a new love. Not long after the outbreak of the war, his wife leaves behind a daughter and her soul ascends to heaven. The daughter is raised by her stepfather and grows into a charming young woman. She and her stepfather's son are childhood sweethearts, innocent and pure. Now that they have both reached adulthood, their love for each other deepens. The stepfather secretly facilitates their union to comfort his beloved wife in the afterlife. Meanwhile, the young man who joined the army returns from the front lines, homeless and wandering the streets, sleeping under the sky and living the life of a "tramp" every day. However, he never ceases to inquire about his beloved daughter. Soon, his wish is fulfilled, but the young man discovers that his daughter lives a prosperous life and has become a wealthy socialite. He is immersed in nature and his heart is filled with unparalleled joy.

Several days later, he leaves this place and heads to the ends of the earth, resuming his life as a "tramp"!

The Most Modern Woman Among Three Modern Women

— Xia Shuxun

A truly modern woman is rational, courageous, and capable of self-reliance. Take Zhou Shuzhen, for example. She is a woman from the petty bourgeoisie, full of reason, bravery, and the ability to support herself. When she is fired from her company, she is not afraid and even says with a smile: "We have our own hands, what are we afraid of? What did God give us hands for? Besides, I am sacrificing myself for the masses!" Indeed, in this bizarre society, as long as a person has hands and is willing to work hard, they won't have trouble finding food everywhere. Although she suffers some material hardship, her spirit remains truly joyful, filled with mutual comfort and understanding.

Therefore, I can boldly say, from a definitive standpoint, that "the most modern person in this film is Zhou Shuzhen, a petty bourgeois woman full of revolutionary spirit." (Unpaid)

Roland Young's Duck Garden on the Summit of Beverly Hills

— Luo Fen

Hollywood star Roland Young has a quirk: he loves ducks most of all. When his friends give him gifts, no matter how precious and valuable they are, he is not particularly surprised. But if you give him a pair of ducks, then he is truly indescribably happy. Therefore, every Christmas, most of the gifts he receives are ducks.

When he first arrived in Hollywood, he co-starred with John Barrymore in "Sherlock Holmes," which was more than fifteen years ago. In these fifteen years, he has bought and received countless ducks from friends. He raises them all carefully in a residence he built on Beverly Hills, which is essentially a duck garden. It has a small reputation in Hollywood, and many people visit it.

Roland Young's quirk has been like this since he was a child. When he was young, his parents took him to the zoo, and he refused to leave when he saw the ducks. Later, his parents bought two ducks to take home, and he finally calmed down. In addition to loving ducks, he also cherishes other animals. Whenever he sees a cat on the road or anywhere else without food, he catches it and carefully feeds it. However, his greatest love is for ducks, which led him to create his unique duck garden.

— Cun

"Call Her Savage" has been completed. Although it is said to be Clara Bow's most successful film since she started making movies, it is still a question whether she will continue to work hard because of its success. Perhaps she will first travel to Europe and take a long rest, and then consider making other films. Her contract with Fox was exaggeratedly described as: "She won't do it unless it's a masterpiece."

Ann Harding Gradually Developing the Intention to Retire

— Ying

Ann Harding's popularity has declined recently. She has stated that after completing the two new films she has already contracted for, she will quit the screen, because she says that being in the film industry has deprived her of all her happiness. Many people in Hollywood also feel that she has often expressed pessimism recently, but some suspect that if her two new films have unexpected success, then her current attitude will disappear. It is unknown whether the guess is correct; only Ann Harding knows for sure.

"The Match King" Story (6)

— Translated by Ximeng

"Paul, Paul," Sonia had apparently succumbed to Paul's hypnotic control. "How much longer must we wait, darling?" "Not much longer, but we must be patient. Does Rodinsky like you?"

"Alas, he doesn't love me very much either. He is very busy with his affairs and has been frowning these days."

"Why?"

"The Ministry of Finance has discovered a deficit of five and a half million. Rodinsky has been running around day and night these days trying to make it up."

Paul jumped up and ran out, grabbing his hat.

"Where are you going?" The woman asked in indescribable horror.

"You can imagine, my dear, that anything that could make me part from you for even a moment must be extremely important."

"Are you coming back?"

"I'll be back in a little while."

"I don't know whether to believe you or not. I suppose you've heard some news from me again and are going to leave me again."

Paul calmly took a ring out of his pocket.

"Darling, this is my mother's wedding ring. In my eyes, it is the most precious thing in the world." He slipped the ring onto Sonia's finger and bowed his head to kiss it gently. "This is my proof."

Sonia looked at the very simple gold ring, her eyes filled with tears of joy.

When Paul Krull went to see Rodinsky, Rodinsky was terrified to be discovered by Paul that his secret had been exposed. He was at a loss for what to do, but he tried to appear calm and said repeatedly, "Krull, are you crazy? You must have heard wrong." But his lips were already turning gray, and trembling frequently, showing his failure, helplessness, surprise, and misery.

Paul, on the other hand, was confident and responded with a slight smile. He knew that victory belonged to him. He stood up. "If you can get your friends in the cabinet to accept my construction, that is, the money they need, fifty million worth of Treasury bonds, are under the pillow on Sonia's bed. This is a small gift from me to you."

Rodinsky said weakly, "You must know that this is extortion."

"Of course," Paul smiled.

"How do you know Sonia?" Rodinsky asked after a long pause, as if gasping for air.

"This is my ability. I know a little about everything. Every great figure in Europe, whether man or woman, I recognize slightly."

Rodinsky pretended to be calm and struck a match to smoke, but his hand was trembling. He said, "Very well, Krull, I can now decide that the Cabinet will definitely grant you the monopoly on matches in Poland." (To be continued)
